# Notice of competition

a.y.2025/26 

for the awarding of 

Scholarships 

Accommodation Service 

Degree Awards 

# UPDATE

# 1. NEW AMOUNTS

Adjusted in line with Managerial Decree 181/2025 scholarship amounts for full-time students (art. 5(1)) 

# 2. SCHOLARSHIP AMOUNT FOR STUDENTS ELIGIBLE FOR A PLACE WHO DO NOT SUBMIT A DECLARATION OF INTEREST OR GIVE IT UP AT CHECK-IN

students who are eligible in the final accommodation service ranking but state that they are not interested in the interest declaration step or do not submit the interest declaration procedure art. 33(2) or give up the place attributed in the “interest declaration outcomes” step (give up the place when the residence is assigned or fail to turn up at the assigned residence on time) To compete for the scholarship amount as a non-resident, they will need to submit the paid housing declaration 

# 3. LEASE UPDATE PROCEDURE(art. 8 par 2)

In the event of a change of accommodation subsequent to submitting the declaration, the student, only and exclusively if he/she is a scholarship winner with a "non-resident" amount, is obliged to communicate the updated data within one month of the registration of the new lease (or stipulation of the same in the case of a different payment basis). This is done via the specific online procedure: "aggiornamento contratto di locazione” (“lease update”) relating to the change of lease and the receipt of registration of the new lease must be attached to guarantee coverage of the minimum period of 10 months. Read art. 8 carefully. 

# 4. SPECIFIC PROVISIONS FOR STUDENTS ATTENDING THE “FILTER SEMESTER” OF MEDICINA E CHIRURGIA, MEDICINA VETERINARIA E ODONTOIATRIA E PROTESI DENTARIA (art 9 par 3)

Students attending the filter semester at a university in Piedmont must apply by 9 September. 

Students attending the filter semester at a non-Piedmont university must submit an application at least to the institution in the region in which they are attending the filter semester and subsequently to EDISU Piemonte, if they are assigned to a Piedmont university or enrol in a related or another course at a Piedmont university. 

All provisions for both types of students are included in art 9(3) and (10) of this notice. 

# 5. SECTION DEDICATED TO EXTRAORDINARY CONTRIBUTIONS FOR STUDENTS WITH A DISABILITY OF 46% OR MORE REGISTERED FOR TARGETED EMPLOYMENT UNDER LAW NO. 68 OF 12 MARCH 1999

For the academic year 2025-26 a special notice will be prepared in October

# GUIDE TO READING THE NOTICE OF COMPETITION

Dear student, 

Here are some pointers that may help you in your reading. 

Each section of the notice of competition is in a different colour: 

SECTION I. RECIPIENTS AND AMOUNTS 

SECTION II. GENERAL PROVISIONS 

SECTION III. SPECIFIC PROVISIONS FOR THE FIRST YEARS 

SECTION IV. SPECIFIC PROVISIONS FOR SUBSEQUENT YEARS 

SECTION V. DEGREE PRIZE 

SECTION VI. PhDs AND SPECIALISATION SCHOOLS 

SECTION VII. SPECIFIC PROVISIONS FOR DISABLED STUDENTS 

SECTION VIII. SPECIFIC PROVISIONS FOR INTERNATIONAL STUDENTS 

SECTION IX. SPECIFIC PROVISIONS FOR THE ACCOMMODATION SERVICE 

SECTION XI. FINAL PROVISIONS 

ATTACHMENTS 

The notice is structured in such a way that you do not have to read it in full. You must read what is contained in sections I “Recipients”, II “General Provisions: Requirements and Submission of the Application” and XI “Final provisions”. You should only read those other sections that interest you according to the type of application you want to submit. 

The text is divided into sections and articles. 

Notes are indicated at the bottom of the page 

Here is a key for the symbols used:

SECTION I 

# RECIPIENTS AND AMOUNTS

# ART. 1 COURSES AND UNIVERSITIES FOR WHICH BENEFITS ARE GRANTED

# Art. 1(1) COURSES

Italian and international students who meet the financial and merit requirements set out in the following articles 6 (general requirements), 9 (first years), 15 (subsequent years), 24 (PhDs and specialisation schools), 29 (students with disabilities) and 30 and 31 (international students), enrolled for the academic year 2025/26 at Piedmont universities identified in the following paragraph, may apply for the scholarship and, if non-resident, the accommodation service in the following types of courses: 

1. bachelor’s degree; 

2. single-cycle master's degree; 

3. master's degree (Ministerial Decree 270/04); 

4. PhD courses (Legislative Decree 210/98) who do not benefit from the scholarship1P; 

5. specialisation schools of at least two years' duration, excluding medical schools under Legislative Decree 368/1999. 

Students enrolled at PhD courses or specialisation schools can apply only for scholarship 

The scholarships relate to the academic year 2025/26. With regard to students enrolled in specialisation schools, scholarships may be granted to those with active enrolment in the relevant academic year of the related school2. 

With regard to scholarships awarded to students enrolled in the additional semester, in addition to the merit and income requirements, enrolment in the current academic year at the time of the application is sufficient, as stipulated in art. 3(5) of Ministerial Decree 1320/2021. Therefore, EDISU (Regional Agency for the Right to Education) will not proceed with the verification of their enrolment for the 2025/26 academic year. 

Students graduating in September 2025 will not be able to apply for a scholarship for the additional semester but only for the degree award if they meet the requirements set out in Section V below. 

Students enrolled at the University of Turin in the joint degrees EAP - Economic Analysis and Policy, LM (MASTER’S DEGREE (Master’s Degree))-56, or EISD - Economics of Innovation for Sustainable Development, LM-56 may participate in this notice of competition, provided that they have not been awarded scholarships granted by the French study support (on the basis of merit and income) or other scholarships granted for similar purposes by the European Community (e.g. Erasmus Mundus Joint Master Degree). If these students only wish to access the canteen service at a reduced cost, they must submit an application in accordance with the Regulations for the Canteen Service, academic year 2025/26. 

Students enrolled at the Polytechnic University of Turin in the Master's Degree Course in Energy and Nuclear Engineering (Turin), pathway SELECT - Environomical Pathways for Sustainable Energy Systems - EIT Joint Programme may participate in this notice of competition, provided they have not been awarded other scholarships granted for similar purposes by the European Community (e.g. Erasmus Mundus Joint Master Degree). If these students only wish to access the canteen service at a reduced cost, they must submit an application in accordance with the Regulations for the Canteen Service, academic year 2025/26. 

Students enrolled in Double Degrees or in international programmes within the Erasmus Mundus Joint Master's initiative whose primary enrolment is at an extended university (lead university) are not eligible to apply for an EDISU scholarship. However, these students will be able to access the canteen at a reduced cost (first bracket) as incoming foreign/exchange students. The university will send EDISU the list of these students they year they attend in Turin, so they do not have to register on EDISU's online services. 

# UPDATE

Art. 9 sets out specific provisions for students attending the “filter semester” of medicina e chirurgia, medicina veterinaria e Odontoiatria e protesi dentaria courses. 

# Art. 1(2) UNIVERSITIES

Students enrolled in Piedmont Universities, SSMLs (Scuole Superiori per Mediatori Linguistici (Language Mediation and Intercultural Communication Schools)), Istituti di alta formazione artistica, musicale e coreutica (Higher Education in Art, Music and Dance Institutions), and ISIAs (Higher Institutes for Artistic Industries) with registered offices in Piedmont (hereinafter referred to as Universities) may apply for the benefits. 

For the academic year 2025/26 students enrolled at the University of Turin, Turin Polytechnic, University of Eastern Piedmont, University of Gastronomic Sciences, Academy of Fine Arts of Turin, Giuseppe Verdi Conservatory of Turin, Language Mediation and Intercultural Communication School of Turin, Cuneo Academy of Fine Arts, European Academy of Media Arts of Novara, “A Vivaldi” Conservatory of Alessandria, “Guido Cantelli” Conservatory of Novara, “G.F. Ghedini” State Conservatory of Cuneo, “A Macagno” Language Mediation and Intercultural Communication School of Cuneo, Novara Musical Theatre School, and IAAD may apply 

# Art. 1(3) COURSE LOCATIONS

All course locations established by the Universities referred to in paragraph 2 above are recognised for the purposes of applying for benefits. 

# Art. 1(4) DISTRIBUTION OF SCHOLARSHIPS AND ACCOMMODATION

The scholarships are funded with revenue from the regional tax for the right to study, regional resources earmarked for the provision of scholarships and other services, (Directorate “Istruzione e Diritto allo studio universitario, Formazione e Lavoro” Sector “Diritto 

allo studio universitario, welfare aziendale e integrazione politiche dell’istruzione,formazione e lavoro”) with state supplementary funds (FIS), resources from the European Social Fund, possible resources from the National Recovery and Resilience Plan PNRR (Next Generation EU project) and sums returned by students in the event of withdrawal3. 

Recipients of scholarships funded with the 2021/2027 European Social Fund $( \mathsf { E S F } + )$ resources will be, first and foremost, female students in subsequent years of STEM courses, then disabled students in subsequent years, and, in the event of residual funds, students in subsequent years of STEM courses with merit requirements as of 10 August 2025 and income requirements, economically disadvantaged students (ISEE indicator less than or equal to half of the maximum reference limit) and, lastly, other students who do not meet the above categories. 

Any NRRP funds are instead reserved for students awarded scholarships as post- $\cdot \mathcal { T } ^ { \mathrm { s t } }$ year students not funded with $\mathsf { E S F + }$ funds. 

The final scholarship rankings are drawn up in such a way as to provide each University with the same percentage of scholarships in relation to eligible applicants, with the exception of doctoral and specialisation school courses for which scholarships are allocated on the basis of the number of applications regularly submitted for the academic year 2025/26 regardless of the requirements. 

The grants are distributed according to the following criteria: 

$1 5 \% ,$ according to the ranking defined in art. 12(1), for students enrolled in the first years of bachelor’s degree, single-cycle master’s degree, master's degree, PhD, and specialisation school courses who submit a Standard Application. Both the winners of the ranking of 7 November 2025 and those of the ranking of 16 December 2025 contribute to the $1 5 \%$ percentage 

2. $8 5 \% ,$ according to the ranking defined in art. 17(1), for enrolled students: 

a. in subsequent years of bachelor’s degree, single-cycle master’s degree, and master's degree courses confirming meritbased benefits (art. 15(1.2)); 

b. in the first years of master's degree courses confirming merit-based benefits (art. 9(1)); 

c. in the subsequent years of bachelor’s degree, single-cycle master’s degree, master's degree, PhD and specialisation school courses who submit a Standard Application (art. 15(1.1) and art. 26(1)). 

The final accommodation service rankings are drawn up in the same way as for the scholarship, in order to distribute the spaces identified in the notice of competition among the Universities, maintaining the same percentage in relation to those entitled and guaranteeing at least one spaces per University. 

For each location, the available spaces are allocated according to the following criteria: 

1. $1 5 \% ,$ according to the ranking defined in art. 12(1), for students enrolled in the first years of bachelor’s degree, single-cycle master’s degree, master's degree courses. The number of places thus identified is further divided by reserving $1 5 \%$ for students with non-EU citizenship with their family residing in a non-EU country and for students with International Protection status, while the remaining $8 5 \%$ is reserved for students with Italian and EU citizenship and for students with non-EU citizenship with their family residing in an EU country. 

2. $8 5 \% ,$ according to the ranking defined in art. 17(1), for enrolled students: 

a. in subsequent years of bachelor’s degree, single-cycle master’s degree, and master's degree courses confirming meritbased benefits (art. 15(1.2)), 

b. in the first years of master's degree courses confirming merit-based benefits (art. 9(1)); 

c. in subsequent years of bachelor’s degree, single-cycle master’s degree, and master's degree courses submitting a Standard Application (art. 15(1.1)). 

There are no places reserved for students enrolled in doctoral courses and specialisation schools. 

# ART. 2 DURATION OF BENEFITS

Benefits may be claimed for the first enrolment at each course level according to the following durations, calculated from the academic year of first enrolment, without prejudice to articles 3 and 9 below. The scholarship may only be applied for once per course year. In the case of course switches or transfers from another university, reference must be made to art. 15(4) below. 

<table><tr><td>Type of course</td><td>Duration of benefits</td></tr><tr><td>Bachelor&#x27;s degree courses</td><td>- FULL-TIME COMMITMENT: three academic years plus a possible additional semester (called the seventh semester)
- PART-TIME COMMITMENT: three academic years</td></tr><tr><td>Single-cycle master&#x27;s degree courses</td><td>- FULL-TIME COMMITMENT: a period equal to the duration of the course stipulated by the respective academic regulations (5 or 6 academic years) plus a possible additional semester
- PART-TIME COMMITMENT: a period equal to the duration of the course stipulated by the respective academic regulations (5 or 6 academic years)</td></tr><tr><td>Master&#x27;s degree courses4</td><td>- FULL-TIME COMMITMENT: two academic years plus a possible additional semester (called the fifth semester)
- PART-TIME COMMITMENT: two academic years</td></tr><tr><td>Research PhDs5 or specialisation schools of at least two years&#x27; duration, excluding medical schools under Legislative Decree 368/1999</td><td>A period equal to the duration of the course as laid down in the respective academic regulations</td></tr></table>

# ART. 3 GROUNDS FOR INELIGIBILITY AND EXCLUSION

Applications that are not completed and submitted in accordance with the terms of this notice of competition will not be considered for the competition. 

The application submission procedures for non-EU or EU international students with their families residing abroad are set out in arts. 30 and 31. 

# Art. 3(1) GROUNDS FOR INELIBIGILITY

The following cases constitute grounds for ineligibility for the benefits. 

Failure to comply with the deadlines for submitting a complete application as set out in this notice of competition in arts. 10(2) (first years), 16(2) (subsequent years), 21 (degree award), 25(3) (PhDs and specialisation schools); 

2. Failure to submit the application online (including in the case of partial or complete online completion of the application) for students completing it with SPID or CIE. 

3. Enrolment in a (first-level) bachelor’s degree course, first-level academic diploma or single-cycle master's degree, while already holding a degree, first-level or second-level academic diploma, specialised or master's degree, single-cycle master's degree, five-year degree6 and university diploma (pre-reform university courses), with the exception of enrolment in a Conservatory or Dance institute in the sole case of enrolment in a bachelor’s degree or master’s degree course. 

Students enrolling in a single-cycle master’s degree course after graduating may only apply for the scholarship from the fourth year of the course (validation of credits for fourth-year scholarship, art. 15(5)). This provision does not apply to students enrolling at the Conservatory 

4. Enrolment in a master’s degree course, while already holding a specialised or master's degree, single-cycle master's degree, five-year degree and university diploma (pre-reform university courses) second-level academic diploma, with the exception of enrolment in a Conservatory or Dance institute in the sole case of enrolment in a bachelor’s degree or master’s degree course. 

5. Enrolment in a doctoral course while having already received a scholarship for a specialisation course, and vice versa, limited to the number of years for which the grant was received. 

6. Enrolment in a doctoral course having already obtained a Specialisation or in a Specialisation course having already obtained a PhD 

7. Being enrolled for the academic year 2025/26 in a course year for which one has already received a grant from EDISU Piemonte or another Italian study support body, unless the student returns the scholarship they have already received by the deadline for scholarship complaints academic year 2025/26. 

8. Enrolment in individual courses. 

9. Enrolment in Conservatory courses for which a high school diploma is not required. 

10. Receiving another similar scholarship7 from public or private institutions, with the exception of scholarships granted by national or foreign institutions aimed at supplementing the training or research activities of scholarship holders by means of travel abroad8. 

11. Having had the benefit referred to in this notice of competition totally withdrawn in previous academic years, with the application of the administrative penalty9. 

12. Having been disqualified from receiving benefits following an economic assessment pursuant to the “EDISU Piemonte Economic Assessment Regulation”. 

13. With regard to the accommodation service request, having had the accommodation service revoked in previous academic years following a measure pursuant to the provisions of the Internal Regulations for University Residences, as amended and supplemented. 

14. With regard to the request for accommodation service, the lack of the requirements for non-resident student status set out in article 4 below 

15. With regard to both the scholarship request and the accommodation service request, having had the EDISU benefits revoked in previous academic years following a measure pursuant to the provisions of the Internal Regulations for University Residences, as amended and supplemented. 

16. With regard to submitting an application for a first year course, enrolment in the first year following course switches or transfers from another university (art. 9(1.1)) 

# Art. 3(2) GROUNDS FOR EXCLUSION

The following cases constitute grounds for exclusion from benefits: 

1. For international students applying with Temporary Access Code academic year 2025/26 (art. 7(1.2)): The absence of the following attachments, which must be submitted online together with the application by the deadline: 

application form, legible and signed by the applicant, in PDF format. The signature must be in pen and in one's own hand or with a qualified electronic (or digital) signature. Word or other signatures are not allowed; 

• front and back copy of the applicant's identity document, legible and valid, in PDF format 

• discrepancy between the declared data and the attached documentation 

2. For international students with their family residing abroad, failure to deliver the required documentation in accordance with the methods and time frames indicated in art. 31(1.1) (first-year students with entry into Italy for enrolment in the academic year 2025/26), 1.2 (first-year students regularly residing in Italy) and 31 para. 1.3 (subsequent-year students) para. 1.5 (PhDs and specialisation schools) and para. 2 (EU students). 

3. False declarations established ex officio10. 

4. Failure to meet the economic requirements set out in art. 6. 

5. The presentation of an ISEE Universitario (ISEE for University) or ISEE per Dottorati (ISEE for PhDs) that do not comply with what is indicated in art. 6. 

6. For students enrolled in years subsequent to the first year of a bachelor’s degree course, single-cycle master’s degree or master's degree course, the lack of the merit requirements set forth in art. 15(2) or, for disabled students, in art. 29(3.2) and Section X for the Extraordinary contribution for students with a disability of $4 6 \%$ or more registered for targeted employment. 

7. Failure to complete and submit complaints online 11if necessary to rectify incorrect data or data modified by EDISU following checks with the Universities during the provisional ranking. Complaints must be submitted by the deadlines and according to the methods identified in arts. 7(6), 12(3) (first years), 17(4) (subsequent years), 22(2) (degree award), 26(3) (PhDs and specialisation schools) and Section X for the Extraordinary contribution for students with a disability of $4 6 \%$ or more registered for targeted employment. 

8. Receipt of similar benefits12 (grants, scholarships, free accommodation...) from other public or private bodies without the students’ having declared that they are opting for one of the benefits (with the exception of scholarships granted by national or foreign institutions to supplement the training or research activities of scholarship holders by means of travel abroad13). 

9. Students who have been awarded an INPS grant or other types of grant for free access (art 5(1) - amount of resident scholarship) or at a reduced rate in any form (art 5(2) - amount of the commuter scholarship) at a university college (Einaudi, Camplus, etc.) are not eligible for a grant with a non-resident amount 

10. Dropping out of studies during the academic year 2025/26 prior to 1 June $2 0 2 6 ,$ as regards successful candidates enrolled in bachelor's degree, master's degree, and single-cycle master’s degree courses. For winners enrolled in a PhD, please refer to art. 24(2). 

11. Transfer to non-Piedmont universities during the academic year 2025/26 (before 1 June 2026). 

12. A transfer from any Italian university or a change of course within one's own university if this results in the non-recognition of the credits necessary to meet the merit requirements of art. 15(2) and (4) or, for disabled students, art. 29(3.2). 

13. The freezing or suspension of the student career during the academic year 2025/26. 

14. Failure to return the scholarship and/or the value of the accommodation service revoked or other benefits or services revoked or other financial complaints in relation to EDISU Piemonte. 

15. With regard to the accommodation service request, having had the accommodation service revoked in previous academic years following a measure pursuant to the provisions of the Internal Regulations for University Residences, as amended and supplemented. 

16. With regard to both the scholarship request and the accommodation service request, having had the EDISU benefits revoked in previous academic years following a measure pursuant to the provisions of the Internal Regulations for University Residences, as amended and supplemented. 

17. As far as the accommodation service is concerned, determination that the student does not meet the requirements of being non-resident pursuant to art. 4 below. 

If EDISU establishes the existence of such grounds for ineligibility or exclusion during checks following the publication of the definitive rankings, the benefits enjoyed will be revoked (art. 38). EDISU will also be able to carry out checks on benefits disbursed in academic years prior to 2025/26 and potentially revoke the benefits (art. 38). 

# ART. 4 “STUDENT TYPE” FOR SCHOLARSHIP PURPOSES

The amount of the scholarship is differentiated according to the following types of students. 

<table><tr><td>RESIDENT</td><td>1. Residents of the municipality in which their course of study is based.
2. Attending distance learning courses run by universities in Piedmont (not to be confused with distance learning because of the pandemic)
3. Subject to detention.
Such students may apply for the scholarship only, without the accommodation service.</td></tr><tr><td>COMPUTER</td><td>Residents in a Municipality other than the one in which their course of study is based, which can be reached by public transport within 60 minutes.
Such students may apply for the scholarship only, without the accommodation service.</td></tr><tr><td>NON-RESIDENT</td><td>Residents in a Municipality other than the one in which their course of study is based, which cannot be reached by public transport within 60 minutes.
Such students may apply for:
1. the accommodation service at EDISU residences and the scholarship;
2. the scholarship alone. Information on the requirements, how and when to obtain the non-resident scholarship-only amount is available in art. 5(1.3) and art. 8(2).
Independent students pursuant to art. 6(1.5) of this notice of competition</td></tr></table>

If students take up or change their official residence after the application for benefits has been submitted, but before 12 November 2025, they must promptly notify EDISU by submitting a ticket; the type of student will be considered on the basis of the new official residence and the date the official residence was changed. The official residence on 12 November 2025 is taken into account in awarding the scholarship. 

On the other hand, in the case of awarding the accommodation service or scholarship with a non-resident amount, students are required to declare their change of residence, even if it is after 12 November 2025. If the change of residence changes the student type, these students lose their non-resident status and the corresponding scholarship amount, which will consequently be recalculated as a commuter amount, for the academic year 2025/26. 

It should be noted that EU and non-EU international students with their families residing entirely abroad maintain their non-resident status regardless of whether or not they take up official residence in Italy, if they submit the declaration of paid residence pursuant to art. 8(2) below. 

EU and non-EU international students enrolled in a doctoral course or specialisation school who take up residence in Italy and apply for EDISU Piemonte benefits by submitting an ISEE Dottorato (PhD ISEE) certificate or ISEE con opzione Nucleo Ristretto (ISEE with “restricted Household” option) will instead be considered on the basis of their residence in Italy. 

If international students take up residency in Italy and this is the same as at least one member of their household (parent, uncle, cousin, sibling, etc.) who generates income of any kind, the type of student will be considered on the basis of the residency taken up in Italy. 

The travel time is calculated using the times defined by the companies operating public transport. These times are transposed by the “Muoversi in Piemonte” system (reference for the Piedmont Region) and similar detection systems such as Google and train timetables at local transport sites. 

The routes taken into account are those between the railway or bus station of the student's municipality of residence and that of the municipality where they are studying, in addition to any walking route connecting two stops. Only those routes are examined that ensure, as quickly as possible, the arrival of students in the municipality where they are studying by 8 a.m. and the return of students to their municipality of residence by 8 p.m. in the evening. For the City of Turin, the reference station is the first arrival/departure station on the route concerned. For the City of Milan, the reference station is the Central Station. 

For the purposes of the calculation, only municipalities are observed and any places and administrative divisions belonging to them are not taken into account. 

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-02-26/96fe0d1f-109c-4be1-a3cb-bd4e5e023921/0d935c0cb1d264e8e334518e3a80d531ea32f97bb1e12045cddba95af6b4123f.jpg)


# ART. 5 SCHOLARSHIP AMOUNTS

The amount of the scholarship14 is determined according to the methods described in the following paragraphs on the basis of the type of student (art. 4) and the ISEE Universitario/Parificato/per Dottorati (University/Equivalent/PhD ISEE) (art. 6). 

Students who have been awarded a scholarship can access EDISU canteens or alternative, EDISU-affiliated services at the tariff corresponding to band 1, which for the academic year 2025/26 amounts to $\notin 3 . 0 0$ for a full meal. Also to students enrolled in the filter semester, referred to in the Legislative Decree of May 15, 2025 No. 71 and the implementation regulations of the new methods of access to single-cycle master's degree programs in Medicina e chirurgia, Medicina veterinaria and Odontoiatria e protesi dentaria, a.y. 2025/26, in case this semester is composed of at least $5 1 \%$ of teaching activities in presence, the discounted rate corresponding to the first bracket of the food service is applied, it is equal to $\notin 3 . 0 0$ for the full meal. 

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-02-26/96fe0d1f-109c-4be1-a3cb-bd4e5e023921/73d9efcfcfc0337b40a0859b1fadb807fb33d8ab8ffc02c6a28e037ec754c21e.jpg)


For students only applying for the additional semester of their course, the amounts and deductions relating to housing and food service fees are halved. 

If all available funds are used up: 

1. students enrolled in years subsequent to the first year, who are eligible in the final scholarship rankings, are eligible15 for a free daily meal in EDISU canteens or alternative services during the calendar year 2026, starting in January. Students who apply for the additional semester of their course can take advantage of the free daily meal until 31 March 2026. In the event of circumstances that prevent the free daily meal (such as participation in international mobility programmes, carrying out internships or other), the value of the meals is not monetised under any circumstances; 

2. students enrolled in the first years who are eligible in the final scholarship rankings may have their meals in EDISU canteens or alternative services at the band 1 rate, which for the academic year 2025/26 is $\notin 3 . 0 0$ for a full meal16; 

3. students applying for the accommodation service who are eligible in the accommodation service and final scholarship ranking are granted, if available, a place in EDISU residences or in residences that have an agreement with the organisation. 

# Art. 5(1) STUDENTS ENROLLED FULL-TIME

The amounts indicated in the following paragraphs have been identified pursuant to art. 3(2), (3) and (5) of Ministerial Decree 1320/2021, the subsequent Circular a 13676 of 11 May 2022 and the Managerial Decree 181/2025 which updated the amounts for the academic year 2025/26 and transposed by the Regional Criteria academic year 2025/26. Pursuant to Annex A of the Regional Criteria, the amounts for students with an ISEE Universitario amounting to between € 23,626.01 and € 26,306.25 are reduced by $5 0 \%$ with respect to those established by Ministerial Decree 204/2023. 

The amounts earmarked for disabled students are indicated in art. 29 of this notice of competition and in Section X of this notice of competition with regard to Extraordinary contributions for students with disabilities of $4 6 \%$ or more registered for targeted employment pursuant to Law no. 68 of 12 March 1999. 

Students awarded a grant for enrolment in a STEM course who transfer to a NON-STEM course, if they continue to meet the requirements, will have the amount recalculated and the second instalment paid with the reduced amount. In the event of winning a NON-STEM scholarship and transferring to a STEM course, the amount will be increased in the second instalment if funds are available. 

The scholarship consists of a cash amount, net of € 150.00 as a contribution towards the catering service at EDISU canteens or alternative services (the amounts below are already calculated net of € 150.00). 


Art. 5(1.1)



RESIDENT STUDENTS

For the purposes of the scholarship amount, “COMMUTER” students also include22: 

students who are successful in the final accommodation service ranking but refuse their place in the online acceptance procedure or fail to submit the acceptance procedure or renounce the place when the residence is assigned (or fail to turn up at the assigned residence on time) and will not be able to submit the paid housing declaration; 

2. students who give up their place after accepting the allocation and checking in, even if they are included in the scrolling ranking. Such students will not be able to make the paid residence declaration; 

3. students who have been awarded an INPS grant or another type of grant for allocation to a university college with payment of part of the tuition fee. 

# Art. 5(1.3)

# NON-RESIDENT STUDENTS23

<table><tr><td colspan="4"></td><td colspan="3">FEMALE STEM COURSE STUDENTS</td></tr><tr><td>ISEE ≤ € 13,153.1224</td><td>€ 13,153.12&lt; ISEE ≤€ 17,537.50</td><td>€ 17,537.50&lt; ISEE ≤€ 23,626.00</td><td>€ 23,626.00&lt; ISEE ≤€ 26,306.25</td><td>ISEE ≤€ 17,537.50</td><td>€ 17,537.50&lt; ISEE ≤€ 23,626.00</td><td>€ 23,626.00&lt; ISEE ≤€ 26,306.25</td></tr><tr><td>€ 7.982,92</td><td>€ 6.922,10</td><td>€ 5.507,68</td><td>€ 3,800.0025</td><td>€ 8.336,52</td><td>€ 6.639,22</td><td>€ 4.093,2626</td></tr></table>

Only students in the following categories are eligible for this scholarship amount: 

1. those who have not requested the accommodation service; 

2. those who have cancelled the accommodation service request by 12:00 p.m. on 9 September 2025; 

3. those who have submitted a “place renunciation” by 12:00 p.m. on 22 September 2025, by means of a complaint against the provisional accommodation service ranking; 

4. those excluded from the final accommodation service ranking for other reasons but successful in the final scholarship ranking. 

5. those eligible in the final accommodation service ranking but state that they are not interested in the interest declaration step or do not submit the interest declaration procedure art. 33(2) or give up the place attributed in the “interest declaration outcomes” step (give up the place when the residence is assigned or fail to turn up at the assigned residence on time) 

6. those eligible in the final accommodation service ranking who were not “allocated” a place in the expression of interest despite having declared their interest, and who therefore cannot benefit from the service due to a lack of available places (art. 33(1) and (2)). 

7. winners or eligible candidates on the final accommodation service ranking, who have completed the acceptance or expression of interest, accepting the place with: 

the Erasmus Option with a foreign stay of 8 months or more (art. 33(4.1)), who must self-certify their cost of residence in accordance with the procedures and time frames indicated in art. 8(2); 

• the Renato Einaudi Option (art. 33(5)), who do not have to self-certify the cost of their residence. 

8. applicants for the accommodation service but attending course locations without EDISU residences, who do not have to submit the expression of interest but only the declaration of paid accommodation. 

9. Independent students in accordance with Article 6(5.1) below. Independent students do not have to submit the declaration of paid accommodation but must enclose the paid rental contract or deed of purchase with their scholarship application. If the independent student does not submit documentation regarding the use of paid accommodation, they will not be considered non-resident for the purposes of the scholarship amount but will receive the commuter amount. 

In order to receive the non-resident scholarship amount, these students must be winners in the final scholarship rankings and have submitted the declaration of paid accommodation (art. 8(2)), with the exception of independent students who must follow the provisions of section 8 above. 

For the students referred to in art. 9(3.2), this scholarship amount will be weighted in relation to the number of months of paid tenancy, provided that it exceeds three. Further information will be provided in the notice of publication of the provisional rankings on 5 March 2026 

If the place is allocated by sliding scale during the year and accepted, this grant amount will have the value of the accommodation service deducted calculated at € 245.45 per month (the month is counted if students enter residence until the $1 5 ^ { \mathrm { t h } }$ day of the month). More information in art. 33(3.1.)

• disbursement of the cash amount, indicated in the table below, net of tax charges 

• allocation of one place for 11 months in EDISU residences or those affiliated with the organisation, the value of which is quantified at $\notin 2 , 7 0 0 . 0 0$ excluding tax

In order to receive the scholarship with the non-resident amount, non-resident students who are not guests of an EDISU residence, whether they are from the EU, non-EU with family in Italy, Europe or a non-EU country, must self-certify their paid residence in accordance with the time frames and procedures indicated in art. 8(2). Otherwise, if they are awarded a grant, they will be paid the amount provided for commuter students. 

For non-EU international first-year students with entry visa for enrolment in academic year 2025/26, the provisions of art. 31(1.1) (Table) apply. 

# Art. 5(2) STUDENTS ENROLLED PART TIME

Students enrolled part time27 in bachelor's, single-cycle master's, and master's degree courses may only benefit from the scholarship, according to the amounts indicated in the table below. 

In order to obtain the relevant amount, non-resident students must self-certify their paid residence in accordance with the procedures and time frames identified in art. 8(2). 

<table><tr><td>Student type</td><td></td></tr><tr><td>Resident</td><td>€ 606.00</td></tr><tr><td>Commuter</td><td>€ 775.00</td></tr><tr><td>Non-resident</td><td>€ 1,409.00</td></tr></table>

On 31 October 2025 (for first-year students of single-cycle bachelor’s degree and master’s degree courses who enrol by 31 October 2025), 30 November 2025 (for first-year and subsequent-year students who enrol by 30 November 2025) and 3 April 2026 (for first-year and subsequent-year students suspended in the December rankings with eligibility to compete in the final April rankings), checks will be carried out on enrolment and type of commitment. Students enrolled on a part-time basis on that date, if they are awarded a scholarship in the definitive rankings, will be paid the amount indicated above and there will be no supplement if, after that date, they change their type of commitment from “part time” to “full time”. 

Scholarship winners with full-time enrolment who change their type of commitment during the academic year will have their scholarship amount recalculated from full-time to part-time with possible partial withdrawal. 

Please remember that the scholarship is exempt from income tax as provided for by Law no. 476 of 13 August 1984 and Circular no. 109/e of 6 April 1995 of the Ministry of Finance and, therefore, the amount received does not have to be included in the IRPEF declarations and does not affect the total amount to be considered a “dependent family member”. It should also be noted that the amount of accommodation service that may be deducted from the gross scholarship amount for non-resident students can be taken as a $1 9 \%$ IRPEF deduction with code 18. 

Section X contains the provisions on “Extraordinary contributions for students with disabilities of $4 6 \%$ or more registered for targeted employment pursuant to Law No. 68 of 12 March 1999”

SECTION II 

# GENERAL PROVISIONS

# ART. 6 ECONOMIC REQUIREMENTS

Students wishing to apply for the benefits provided for in this notice of competition must meet the financial requirements set out below when submitting their application. 

# Art. 6(1) ECONOMIC REQUIREMENTS (ISEE UNIVERSITARIO, ISEE PARIFICATO, ISEE DOTTORATO E ISEE NUCLEO RISTRETTO)

Students’ economic circumstances are identified, with regard to ISEE, by the Prime Ministerial Decree 159/2013, art. 10 of Legislative Decree 147/2017, the regulatory amendments introduced respectively by Decree-Law 4/2019, Decree-Law 34/2019 and Ministerial Decree 347/2019, as well as based on the additional selection criteria implementing art. 3 of Ministerial Decree 1320/2021 and art. 5 of Prime Ministerial Decree 09/04/2001 and arts. 7 and 8 of Legislative Decree 68/2012. 

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-02-26/96fe0d1f-109c-4be1-a3cb-bd4e5e023921/00255b5dafc69f4f43e137e3f27cfaf3d73fcf8a199c29c27e7e40904161c228.jpg)


The information below must NOT be considered in any way as a substitute for the regulations in force regarding completing the ISEE Universitario (Prime Ministerial Decree 159/2013, art. 10 of Legislative Decree 147/2017, the regulatory amendments introduced respectively by Decree-Law 4/2019, Decree-Law 34/2019 and Ministerial Decree 347/2019 and Prime Ministerial Decree 09/04/2001). 

To be able to apply for the benefits provided by EDISU Piemonte such as a scholarship, accommodation service, and degree awards, students must possess the following when filling out the application: 

• a ISEE Universitario certificate without observations regarding omissions/ discrepancies. In the event that the ISEE Universitario has observations regarding omissions/discrepancies, EDISU Piemonte requires that the documentation proving the correctness of the contents of the DSU be sent, as indicated in the INPS and Ministry of Labour message no. 8415 of 26/10/2020. 

• the receipt certifying the submission and signing of the DSU at the CAAF (Authorised Tax Assistance Centre) without the related processing of the certificate by INPS; 

OR 

in the case of an Italian, EU or non-EU student whose family resides partly or entirely abroad and who requires the calculation of the ISEE Parificato: 

• consular documentation as required in art. 30 below 

The ISEE Universitario required for applying for a scholarship academic year 2025/26 must be valid, i.e. it must be signed starting from 01 January 2025. 

The 2025 ISEE Universitario (hereinafter ISEE Universitario) or the calculation of the ISEE Parificato of the household may not exceed the limit of € 26,306.25. 

However, students for whom the Equivalent Asset Situation Indicator (hereinafter referred to as ISPE, equivalent to the indicator called ISPEUP if calculating the ISEE Parificato) exceeds the limit of € 57,187.53 are excluded from the benefits provided for in this notice of competition.28 

The ISPE is calculated by dividing the Asset Situation Indicator (hereinafter referred to as ISP) or the Asset Situation Indicator supplemented with the criteria of Prime Ministerial Decree 9 April 2001 (hereafter referred to as ISPU) for the equivalence scale (SE) indicated in the ISEE Universitario/Parificato. 

<table><tr><td rowspan="3">Requirements</td><td>INCOME</td><td>ASSETS</td></tr><tr><td>ISEE Universitario</td><td>ISPE</td></tr><tr><td>≤ € 26,306.25</td><td>≤ € 57,187.53</td></tr></table>

Students applying for scholarships and, if non-resident, accommodation service for the academic year 2025/26 MUST have, under penalty of exclusion from the competition, a ISEE Universitario certificate or complete consular documentation (arts. 6(5), (30) and (31)). 

Please note that, for the purpose of retrieving the ISEE Universitario data, EDISU Piemonte will download the last certificate present in the INPS database for the year 2025 online. 

The ISEE Universitario/Parificato certificate must, therefore, be signed in the year 2025. 

• If submitting the ISEE Universitario, the relevant DSU must be signed by the application deadline and must relate to income earned in the 2023 tax year and assets owned as at 31 December 2023. In the event that the ISEE Universitario has observations regarding omissions/discrepancies, EDISU Piemonte requires that the documentation proving the correctness of the contents of the DSU be sent, as indicated in the INPS and Ministry of Labour message no. 8415 of 26/10/2020. 

• If calculating the ISEE Parificato for international EU students only, including Italian students without residence in Italy, the consular documentation must be delivered within the deadlines indicated in article 31(2) and (3) and must only relate to income 

earned in the 2023 tax year and assets owned as of 31 December 2023 (for further information, please refer to the section on international students, arts. 30 and 31). 

• If calculating the ISEE Parificato for international non-EU students only, the consular documentation must be delivered within the deadlines indicated in article 31(1) and (3), and must only relate to income earned in the 2024 tax year and assets owned as of 31 December 2024 (for further information, please refer to the section on international students, arts. 30 and 31). 

For students enrolled in a doctoral course or specialisation school, please refer to section VI art. 24 of this notice of competition for further specifications. 

Students of Medicina e chirurgia, Medicina veterinaria and Odontoiatria e protesi dentaria courses who do NOT attend the filter semester in Piedmont but who subsequently enrol in Piedmont must be in possession of the 2025 ISEE Universitario Certificate they submitted for the 2025-26 scholarship application with the agency for the right to education in the region where they attended the filter semester.
