![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-02-26/96fe0d1f-109c-4be1-a3cb-bd4e5e023921/afb5aa1dec23cc197937586ea3be1fe293601864348d3591412418155b92cf15.jpg)


Students under international protection or stateless persons must be in possession of an ISEE Universitario that will take into account any income and assets produced and/or owned in Italy. These students do not have to refer to their family of origin as their household is resident in Italy and is made up of the applicants for benefits and any other persons present in their registered family status. 

FOR UKRAINIAN STUDENTS ONLY WITH FAMILY ENTIRELY ABROAD AND WITH A TEMPORARY RESIDENCE PERMIT 

Pursuant to and in accordance with art. 274h(395) of Budget Law No. 213/2023, Temporary Residence Permits are extended until 31 December 2025. 

Students from Ukraine holding a temporary residence permit do NOT have to submit the ISEE Universitario or any consular documents relating to their family of origin. They are only required to send the documents relating to the part of the family present in Italy with whom they may reside to EDISU Piemonte according to the methods identified in art. 31(1) of this Notice of competition. These documents include: the identity document and copy of the residence permit of all the family members and any current account balance, including average balance as of 31 December 2024, for the processing of the ISEE Parificato by the EDISU Piemonte CAAF operators. 

For non-EU or EU international students with family wholly or partly resident abroad, the provisions of art. 30 of this notice of competition apply. 

# Art. 6(1.2) INCOME ACCRUED IN THE 2023 TAX YEAR FOR ISEE CALCULATION

For the purposes of determining the ISEE Universitario, any declared or assimilated income received in the 2023 tax year must be considered, as well as any other tax-exempt income component, including scholarships and all EDISU contributions received in the 2023 tax year (with the exception of support for disabled students and reimbursements for regional tax or travel expenses), parttime collaborations with EDISU, Universities or other Bodies, income from employment abroad exclusively taxed in the foreign country, child support payments actually received, welfare, social security and allowances (not already included in total income). 

Only non-EU international students must also refer to income received in the year 2024 to determine the calculation of the ISEE Parificato (for more information, please refer to the section on international students, art. 30 below). 

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-02-26/96fe0d1f-109c-4be1-a3cb-bd4e5e023921/61a56f53e3f4160e638f0835156e92127cd86a88c5a721f25864bbfbff69d67a.jpg)


Pursuant to the Council of State's Ruling of 29 February 201630, it is noted that amounts deriving from disability INDEMNITY are NOT to be considered INCOME and therefore should NOT be indicated in the DSU. 

For the purposes of completing the ISEE Universitario/Parificato statement, the income received by all members of the household must be declared for ISEE Univesitario/Parificato purposes even in the case of exemption from the obligation to submit a tax return and the same is not subject to IRPEF. 

For the purpose of determining the Asset Situation Indicator (ISP), the amount of movable assets (including the average stock) and immovable assets of all the members of the household for ISEE Universitario/Parificato purposes as at 31/12/2023 must be indicated31; non-EU students must instead refer to the date of 31/12/2024 (please refer to the section on international students, art. 30 below). 

# Art. 6(1.3) SCHOLARSHIP AMOUNTS RECEIVED IN THE 2023 TAX YEAR FOR ISEE CALCULATION

For the purpose of calculating the ISEE for subsidised benefits for the right to university study to apply for a scholarship and, if nonresident, the accommodation service, the amount of the scholarship from EDISU Piemonte or another body for the right to university study, received in the 2023 tax year, is subsequently deducted by the Granting Body, dividing it by the equivalence scale and then subtracting the result of this division from the previously calculated ISEE value. NO amounts relating to other contributions granted by EDISU or scholarship amounts received by other household members for ISEE purposes in the same tax year other than the benefit applicant may be deducted. 

Non-EU international students who are required to submit income for the 2024 tax year must also indicate any scholarship amount received in the 2023 tax year when calculating the ISEE Parificato. 

# Art. 6(1.4) HOUSEHOLD FOR ISEE PURPOSES

It is advisable to check the composition of one's household by means of a family status certificate updated at the time of applying for the scholarship, and to go to the CAAF for completing a new ISEE Universitario/Parificato certificate if there is a discrepancy. 

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-02-26/96fe0d1f-109c-4be1-a3cb-bd4e5e023921/d6c9e497615c4eaa9576f111dc4999401f8e45db3baf0f18f41b01845557138f.jpg)


Please note that the household for ISEE Universitario purposes is defined primarily on the basis of the registered household, to which any components such as the spouse with a different residence or registered with AIRE, as well as the natural parent not cohabiting with the recognised child, must be added. It is, therefore, of the utmost importance to make one's family situation explicit when signing the DSU, since it is the initial and fundamental element for defining the DSU and is one of the few elements that is still selfdeclared based on Presidential Decree 445/2000. 

If a student no longer has a relationship with one of their parents, appropriate documentation must be produced to prove the economic and emotional estrangement of the parent no longer cohabiting with the student in order to obtain the ISEE Universitario/Parificato. Such rulings or reports must be issued by the competent court or by the Offices of the Social Services of the Municipality where the household living with the student is registered (or by an equivalent foreign institution in the case of international students). 

Students holding international protection or stateless persons do NOT have to refer to their family of origin, but they must indicate that their household resides in Italy and that it is made up of the applicants for benefits and any other persons present in the registered family. 

Such students must be in possession of a ISEE Universitario that will take into account any income and assets produced and/or owned in Italy. In the event that the ISEE Universitario has observations regarding omissions/discrepancies, EDISU Piemonte requires that the documentation proving the correctness of the contents of the DSU be sent, as indicated in the INPS and Ministry of Labour message no. 8415 of 26/10/2020. 

# FOR UKRAINIAN STUDENTS ONLY WITH FAMILY ENTIRELY ABROAD AND WITH A TEMPORARY RESIDENCE PERMIT

Pursuant to and in accordance with art. 274h(395) of Budget Law No. 213/2023, Temporary Residence Permits are extended until 31 December 2025. 

Students from Ukraine holding a temporary residence permit do NOT have to submit the ISEE Universitario or any consular documents relating to their family of origin. They are only required to send the documents relating to the part of the family present in Italy with whom they may reside to EDISU Piemonte according to the methods identified in art. 31(1) of this Notice of competition. 

These documents include: the identity document and copy of the residence permit of all the family members and any current account balance, including average balance as of 31 December 2024, for the processing of the ISEE Parificato by the EDISU Piemonte CAAF operators. 

# Art. 6(1.5) “INDEPENDENT STUDENT” HOUSEHOLD

In order to be granted the scholarship, students constitute an independent household32 from that of their family of origin if both of the following requirements are met: 

• residence outside the housing unit of the family of origin, for at least two actual years from the date of submission of the application, in housing not owned by a member of the family; 

• presence of adequate personal income 3 3 received in the tax years $2 0 2 3$ and 2024 not less than € 9,000.00 35 for each year. This amount includes any tax-declared or assimilated income or self-employment income received in the tax years 2023 and 2024, as well as any other tax-exempt income components, income from employment abroad exclusively taxed in the foreign country, child support payments actually received, welfare, social security and indemnity payments (not already included in total income). 

When filling out the application for benefits, to confirm their status, the independent student is required to enclose the rental contract or deed of ownership of their home, even if it is encumbered by a mortgage. 

If the independent student does not submit documentation regarding the use of paid accommodation, they will not be considered non-resident for the purposes of the scholarship amount but will receive the commuter amount. 

In all cases where students, although no longer living with their family of origin, do not meet the requirements to be considered independent, reference is made to their parents' income and assets in accordance with current legislation. 

In the event that married students do not meet the threshold for suitable income required for independent status, their spouse's personal income36 received in tax years 2023 and 2024 must be taken into account. If the latter also does not reach the minimum amount of € 9,000.00, the requirement can be met by adding the student's income with that of their spouse.37 Therefore, the DSU will only refer to the household that students have formed with their spouse, excluding their family of origin. In all other cases where the personal income received does not reach the required minimum limit for the 2023 and 2024 tax years (€ 9,000.00 for each year), students must refer to their family of origin, thus excluding their spouse and any children. 

If independent students are found to be living with other persons in their registered family status, the income of all the persons in the registered household, even if there are no family ties, must be taken into account. 

Please note: students enrolled in a doctoral course or specialisation school cannot apply for benefits as independent students since this case only applies to the ISEE Universitario and not to the ISEE Dottorato. Please refer to article 24(3) below. 

SEPARATE or DIVORCED students, even if they have children, but WITHOUT the requirements for independent student status, must compulsorily do the ISEE Universitario with their family of origin (paragraph 1.4). 

# Art. 6(1.6) CASES WITH A HOUSEHOLD COMPOSED OF JUST THE STUDENT

Students who do not qualify as independent may in any case submit a ISEE Universitario relating solely to their economic status if they are orphans or if they are in a registered partnership, as described in section 1.7 below. 

Care Leavers as well as students who are in the care of social services or have a court-ordered removal order issued by a Judge constitute a household unto themselves. 

The application must be accompanied by appropriate documentation proving the student's circumstance; for any information or support in filling in the application, students may open a ticket in the ISEE economic requirements section of the system. 

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-02-26/96fe0d1f-109c-4be1-a3cb-bd4e5e023921/0adc8b1e15e73a25f08d3c8fc27b1b07b04846fd5986638852ab41581de10ea6.jpg)


Definition of registered cohabitation: a group of persons normally cohabiting for religious, care, military or punishment reasons and having their residence at the same address (religious institution, nursing home, barracks, prison, etc.). 

In all cases where students meet the requirements of art. 5 of Presidential Decree 223/89, they may apply to have the ISEE Universitario certificate in registered cohabitation issued by presenting appropriate documentation proving their status to the CAAF and, subsequently, to EDISU Piemonte. 

The categories envisaged for registered cohabitation are: 

belonging to a religious order; 

• military; 

• host communities; 

• subjected to detention. 

In the event that the student who is in a registered cohabitation (military, host community, or subject to detention) is “MARRIED”, they must refer to the household of their spouse and any children, as described in section 1.4 above, for the purpose of preparing the ISEE Universitario certificate. If the applicant and their minor child live in the registered cohabitation, the latter must be considered a member of the parent's household (see the document “List of certifications to be attached to the application for students with a student-only household, international protection seekers and the disabled” available in the “Scholarships > attachments” section of the EDISU website). 

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-02-26/96fe0d1f-109c-4be1-a3cb-bd4e5e023921/029ba079efd634eb85ea022dea0a94dc5f62e824e54fe7d8c76550e90b072084.jpg)


# Art. 6(2) ECONOMIC REQUIREMENTS WITH SUBMISSION OF ISEE UNIVERSITARIO

To apply for a scholarship and, if non-resident, for accommodation service, students must apply for an ISEE certificate that applies to the Facilitated Benefits for the Right to University Study (hereinafter referred to as ISEE Universitario)38 in respect of students applying for benefits, at an Authorised Tax Assistance Centre (CAAF), or, if they have the SPID, by connecting to the INPS website39. Please note that, in order to obtain the ISEE Universitario, it is mandatory to fill in box C (University Benefits) of the Single Self-Declaration (Dichiarazione Sostitutiva Unica, DSU). In the event that the ISEE Universitario has observations regarding omissions/discrepancies, EDISU Piemonte requires that the documentation proving the correctness of the contents of the DSU be sent, as indicated in the INPS and Ministry of Labour message no. 8415 of 26/10/2020. 

You may fill in the application for EDISU benefits if you have a ISEE Universitario certificate for the person applying for benefits, or with only the receipt attesting to the signing of the DSU at the CAAF40 without the relative processing of the certificate by INPS. 

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-02-26/96fe0d1f-109c-4be1-a3cb-bd4e5e023921/ce2a0f0726918d9b151403dc24555794532049417960ea2421a66eb9c4eb6e20.jpg)


Please note that the issue of the ISEE Universitario is NOT immediate. On the basis of the information contained in the DSU and other information collected at INPS and the Italian Revenue Agency, a certificate containing the ISEE calculation and the information used to obtain it will be issued within ten working days. Therefore, in order to have the ISEE Universitario within the deadline for complaints (art. 7(6)), you should not contact the CAAF in the days immediately preceding the deadlines for requesting the benefits indicated in the following Notice of competition to sign the DSU. 

EDISU Piemonte is NOT in any way responsible for the failure to transmit the data contained in the DSU and/or processing of the ISEE Universitario for the application for the benefits referred to in this Notice of competition. 

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-02-26/96fe0d1f-109c-4be1-a3cb-bd4e5e023921/2533d123a33c929e199b481fc226275f94ce45fdba386e70b3079aaae1691329.jpg)


# Art. 6(2.1) NON-ACCEPTANCE OF THE ISEE CERTIFICATE BY EDISU PIEMONTE

Please note that for the application for benefits relating to the academic year 2025/26 EDISU Piemonte will verify that the ISEE Certificate applies to the Benefits for the Right to University Study in respect of the applicant. 

# Students will be listed as “excluded” in the provisional ranking when:

• the data of the ISEE certificate or the Single Self-Declaration are not available in the INPS database. The data can only be rectified if the applicant has a valid DSU for the right to study, signed before the deadline for applying for benefits; 

• the last ISEE Certificate in the INPS database is not valid for the right to university study for the benefit applicant. The data can only be rectified if the applicant has a valid ISEE certificate for the right to study, processed by INPS by the deadline for complaints relating to the benefit requested; 

• the certificate is found to have an ISEE value that cannot be calculated, and therefore no certificate or DSU was found in the INPS database by the expiry date of the benefit application. The data cannot be rectified. 

It is the students’ responsibility to verify any reasons for the non-availability or non-calculability of the ISEE Universitario certificate and to promptly correct them within the deadline. 

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-02-26/96fe0d1f-109c-4be1-a3cb-bd4e5e023921/4d6a2a90b1bf39b3a03bc78e601c41a3a9d81d6c5b91de7804104b94fb53e9b0.jpg)


EDISU Piemonte is not responsible for the non-availability or non-calculability of the ISEE Universitario certificate. 

For the purpose of retrieving the ISEE Universitario data, EDISU Piemonte will download the last certificate present in the INPS database for the year 2025 online. It must, therefore, be checked that the last ISEE processing request is valid for the right to university study for the applicant for EDISU Piemonte benefits, i.e. by filling in box C in the relevant DSU, and does not have any observations regarding omissions/discrepancies. If an ISEE certificate valid for the right to university study has not been requested, it must be requested by completing this box in the DSU by the application deadline for the academic year 2025/26. 

Following the online retrieval of ISEE data, students will receive a receipt containing the ISEE data retrieved from the INPS database. The same shall be sent within 48 working hours of receipt of the e-mail with the subject line “Receipt of file” as described in art. 7(1.1) and (2) below. The receipt entitled “INPS Data Receipt” may contain: 

• the summary of the ISEE Universitario-Equivalence Scale-ISP values deriving from the last ISEE Universitario certificate found in the INPS database and the relative recalculation carried out automatically for the purposes of the request; 

• any notice of non-acceptance of the same certificate for the purposes of the competition, i.e.: the non-validity of the ISEE for the right to university study for the person requesting the benefits, the failure to find data relating to the ISEE certificate due to the absence of valid certificates in the INPS database; 

If an ISEE, even an ISEE Universitario, is found that contains observations regarding an “omission or discrepancy”, in the INPS Data receipt, the students will be required to transmit the documentation proving the correctness of the contents of the DSU, as indicated in the INPS and Ministry of Labour message no. 8415 of 26/10/2020. Documentation may be submitted via the Data modification procedure by 12:00 p.m. on 9 September 2025, the application deadline, or later via the ticketing system, ISEE economic requirements section. It is also possible to submit a new ISEE Universitario Certificate that rectifies the omissions/ discrepancies found in the previous one. 

In the event that the automatic search for the last ISEE statement processed for the year 2025 in the INPS database does not produce any results, students will still be sent the receipt entitled “INPS Data”. In it, however, the failure to find the ISEE certificate data will be specified. In this case, EDISU Piemonte will regularly query the INPS database until the deadline for the benefit complaint. If an ISEE certificate processed in the year 2024 is found by that date, students will then receive a new “INPS Data” receipt containing, however, a summary of the ISEE-SE-ISP values found and/or any notice of non-acceptance. Otherwise, students will be excluded in the provisional ranking. 

If students, when completing the online application in the appropriate box in the economic data section, have indicated a scholarship amount received in the 2023 tax year, the amount will be automatically deducted. This sum must also be indicated in the DSU under exempt income (box FC4). Students will be included in the definitive ranking with the ISEE and ISPE indicators, recalculated net of the grant amount entered, relating to the last valid certificate for Right to University Study benefits. The “INPS Data” receipt described above will show the recalculated ISEE and ISPE values. 

Students who find themselves in possession of an “INPS Data” receipt that indicates the non-acceptance or failure to find the ISEE certificate, may enter new economic data considered valid for the competition by means of the data modification procedure by the deadline of the application for benefits, as described subsequently in art. 7(5), or, after the deadline of the application, by submitting a formal complaint as described subsequently in article 7(6). 

# Art. 6(3) ISEE CORRENTE (CURRENT ISEE)

If there are significant changes in income as a result of adverse events (e.g. loss of job, suspension or reduction of work activity or interruption of social welfare benefits) or a reduction in assets, INPS offers citizens the possibility to calculate a ISEE Corrente41 based on the income of the last twelve months (or two months in the case of a permanent employee) and, from 1 April of each year, on the assets held as at 31 December of the year preceding the DSU (31 December 2023). The ISEE Corrente may also be issued following a significant change in the household's income, greater than $2 5 \%$ or in the event of a reduction in assets of more than $2 0 \% ^ { 4 2 } ,$ compared to the income or asset situation identified in the ISEE calculated according to the ordinary rules. Before requesting the calculation of the ISEE Corrente, an ISEE certificate, calculated according to the ordinary rules, must already have been issued. 

The ISEE Corrente must be valid on the date of submission of the application for the benefit requested (or on the date of submission If only incomes are updated, the ISEE Corrente [Current ISEE] is valid for six months from the time of submission of this DSU, unless there are changes in the employment situation or in the receipt of benefits, in which case the ISEE Corrente must be updated within two months of the change. If only assets or assets and income are updated, the ISEE Corrente is valid until 31 December 2025. If during the ISEE CORRENTE validity period, in which the income component has been updated, or only this, changes occur in the employment situation or in the receipt of benefits, the ISEE Corrente must be updated within two months of the change. If the ISEE corrente certificate is the latest one in the INPS database, it will be retrieved electronically (section 2.2 above): it is the student's responsibility to check the data in the “INPS data receipt” and, if there are any anomalies, to proceed with the modification of the economic data using the appropriate procedures. 

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-02-26/96fe0d1f-109c-4be1-a3cb-bd4e5e023921/320ca43d8fe4d0390717a046d628c9fab449d7ae756c45d2ee72bee676053077.jpg)


Students in receipt of a reduced scholarship whose financial situation has deteriorated since the declaration submitted when the grant was awarded may submit appropriate documentation to recalculate the amount of the second scholarship instalment by submitting the ISEE Corrente. 

# Art. 6 para. 4 ISEE FOR PhD COURSES

The household of students resident in Italy enrolled exclusively in PhD courses or specialisation schools may ONLY be made up of the applicants themselves and any spouses, children under the age of 18 (nucleo RISTRETTO, RESTRICTED household)43, as well as children over the age of 18, without prejudice to the possibility for beneficiaries to form the household according to the ordinary 44 rules 

It should be noted that the ISEE nucleo RISTRETTO may also be requested by students enrolled in PhD courses or specialisation schools whose registered household is made up of their family of origin. In this case, an explicit request must be made to the CAAF when completing the DSU by filling in box A “RESTRICTED HOUSEHOLD”. Please note that in order to take advantage of the “Nucleo Ristretto” (Restricted Household) option, interested students must sign the DSU for the issue of the ISEE certificate as “declarant”. Please note that students enrolled in PhD courses or specialisation schools residing abroad must present an ISEE Parificato certificate, and therefore will not be able to take advantage of the “restricted household” option. 

Students enrolled in a doctoral course or specialisation school are invited to consult Section VI of this notice of competition in order to obtain all specific information. 

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-02-26/96fe0d1f-109c-4be1-a3cb-bd4e5e023921/ca2eabc96550fe874ac911f04f76375637a1a8aa88a8705741ab486855f11d18.jpg)


The above information is NOT to be considered in any way a substitute for the regulations in force regarding the completion of the ISEE Universitario (Prime Ministerial Decree 159/2013). 

Students enrolled in doctoral courses or specialisation schools are advised that the ISEE and ISPE thresholds are the same as those indicated in Article 6(1) above 

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-02-26/96fe0d1f-109c-4be1-a3cb-bd4e5e023921/df9a286c5e4d6ed26922448705a35812fa7975c2cc5bac1e8dbdfd3597ad0b3c.jpg)


# Art. 6(5) ECONOMIC REQUIREMENTS FOR CALCULATION OF ISEE PARIFICATO

The ISEE Parificato takes into account income generated and assets owned abroad even by household members who are not resident in Italy. 

EDISU Piemonte only accepts the ISEE Parificato drawn up by the operators of affiliated CAAFs and calculated directly in EDISU. Even if valid, ISEE Parificato certificates handed in by students and processed c/o CAAF offices, even if affiliated with the organisation, will not be accepted under any circumstances. 

For the calculation of the ISEE Parificato, it is compulsory to submit consular documentation, translated and legalised in accordance with the regulations in force, relating to the composition of the household, and the income produced and assets held abroad by all the members of the household (for more information, please refer to article 30). 

The Equivalent indicator is issued exclusively by the CAAFs affiliated with EDISU Piemonte present in EDISU Piemonte premises, which will process the ISEE Parificato following the compliant evaluation of the consular documentation. Please note that the evaluation of consular documentation and the processing of the calculation of the ISEE Parificato will only be visible to students when the provisional or definitive ranking of the benefit applied for is published; therefore, it is very important to carefully read the list of consular documentation contained in art. 30, l’Allegato E for international students and, in case of doubt, it is advisable to contact the EDISU offices through the ticketing system. 

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-02-26/96fe0d1f-109c-4be1-a3cb-bd4e5e023921/67f54b2a7e6f62b5154cba84e90a044711d2253d2e5bb7adaca7654b8039c30f.jpg)


Please note that consular documentation will not be evaluated through the ticketing system and that offices are only required to provide information. 

Non-EU and EU international students with a household not resident in Italy must follow the provisions of art. 30 and 31. 

These directives also apply to Italian students whose household members (all or some of them) reside abroad without being registered with AIRE (Register of Italians Resident Abroad), as well as in the case of a household wholly resident abroad. Students in this situation are invited to refer to paragraph 5.1 below for further details on the documentation required and the method of submitting the application for benefits. 

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-02-26/96fe0d1f-109c-4be1-a3cb-bd4e5e023921/08c89ea037e16d664920cd9a223cf5532dc674e3ada47d36fa6088ff88b89edf.jpg)


The AIRE is regulated under art. 27 of Presidential Decree 223/89 and contains the data of Italian citizens residing abroad for a period of more than twelve months. This registration, which is not compulsory, entails the cancellation of national residence, so if both parents are registered there, the economic and asset situation of the household must be reported in the ISEE Parificato. 

Please note that the consular documentation must be sent to EDISU Piemonte, under penalty of definitive exclusion from the competition: 

• according to the timetable and methods described in article 31 below for non-EU and EU international students; 

• according to the time frames and methods described in paragraph 5.1 below for students with Italian citizenship (including students with dual citizenship who use Italian citizenship). 

The ISEE Parificato is calculated by EDISU exclusively for internal use and only once the documentation has been assessed as suitable and complete. The ISEE Parificato is not calculated in case of incomplete or inadequate documentation, nor can it be used to apply for benefits outside of EDISU, unless otherwise specified by official regulations. 

The ISEE Parificato is calculated on the basis of the data obtained from the first complete and correct documentation received by EDISU: no further documentation on incomes and assets will be accepted in order to vary the value of the ISEE Parificato already calculated by EDISU. 

If a student believes that the ISEE Parificato calculation carried out by EDISU does not reflect the real economic situation of their family and that there have been errors in its calculation, they may communicate this exclusively through the complaints procedure (art. 7 paragraph 6). For this reason, too, students are invited to submit their documentation by the deadlines indicated in art. 31, paragraphs 1, 2 and 3, so that their ISEE value can be displayed in the provisional ranking. 

# Art. 6 paragraph 5.1 SPECIFICATIONS FOR STUDENTS WITH ITALIAN CITIZENSHIP WHO NEED TO CALCULATE THE ISEE PARIFICATO

Italian students (including students with dual citizenship who use their Italian citizenship) who need to calculate the ISEE Parificato must submit all the consular documentation indicated in article 30, paragraph 3, under penalty of exclusion from the competition. Please note that in the case of students with Italian citizenship, the documents relating to the income produced by the household both in Italy and abroad must only refer to the 2023 tax year, and to the date of 31/12/2023 as regards assets. 

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-02-26/96fe0d1f-109c-4be1-a3cb-bd4e5e023921/f4eaf163620b2bbe1849e709c48f45ca9da3d324db649896872cd199169f5259.jpg)


It should be noted that students with Italian citizenship are also required to have foreign consular documentation legalised and translated into Italian if the document has been drawn up in another language. For further information in this regard, students are invited to carefully consult article 30, paragraph 3 below. This documentation must be submitted to EDISU Piemonte by the application deadline 

Italian students (including students with dual citizenship who use Italian citizenship) who are required to calculate the ISEE Parificato must submit documentation on the composition of their household, foreign income and assets using the attachment procedure available when completing the online application. Students must therefore attach consular documentation (both the original language version and the version translated into Italian) relating to the composition of their household and to income and assets produced/possessed (both in Italy and abroad) by the student's household via the online procedure and by the application deadline, under penalty of exclusion from the competition. 

If students are resident in Italy, before submitting their application for a scholarship and/or accommodation service, they must sign a DSU to request an ordinary ISEE containing the data of their household in Italy, which will subsequently be supplemented with the data relating to their family of origin. These data are calculated on the basis of the above-mentioned consular documentation, which must be translated and legalised in accordance with current legislation. The ordinary ISEE certificate must be attached to the scholarship application together with the required consular documentation. 

If the ordinary ISEE is absent by the deadline for the application for benefits, the copy of the certificate and any missing consular documents for the calculation of the ISEE Parificato must be transmitted by the students by means of a complaint procedure, in accordance with the methods indicated in article 7, paragraph 6 below. 

Once the online application has been completed and submitted, the attached consular documentation will be examined by EDISU Piemonte operators and students will see the outcome of the evaluation of the documentation in the ranking. 

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-02-26/96fe0d1f-109c-4be1-a3cb-bd4e5e023921/46e249c3d2ed1ee50eb61c43b54fa60ea8a10d6df0b99ddb1dbb0fa14f5f9399.jpg)


For the evaluation to be published in the provisional ranking, it must be received by EDISU by the deadline for the online application (9 September 2025, 12:00 p.m.). If the documentation is received after this deadline but before the deadline for submitting complaints, the evaluation will be published directly in the definitive ranking, without the possibility of submitting further complaints. Therefore, students are invited to send in their documentation in advance, so that the provisional outcome of the assessment can be seen. 

In the event of a negative outcome of the consular documentation assessment, students may submit missing/corrected documentation in accordance with the provisions of article 7, paragraph 5.1 and 6.1 below. 

After the new documentation has been received at EDISU via attachment in the online complaint procedure, the new outcome will be published in the definitive ranking. 

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-02-26/96fe0d1f-109c-4be1-a3cb-bd4e5e023921/5ab2731cb9bacff8899c59f11a48be7bc84f2d76288d3fb912e79d185ea7436e.jpg)


The procedure for uploading the required documentation involves uploading a maximum of 5 attachments in .pdf version, each no larger than 1MB. Students must combine the different types of documents in a single file, e.g. a single file containing the ordinary and ISEE Parificato, another containing the composition of the household and any divorce decrees or death certificates, another containing all the income received by the household and one relating to movable assets (current accounts, savings, deposits, etc.) and real estate (buildings expressed in square metres). 

# ART. 7 HOW TO SUBMIT AN APPLICATION

(Non-EU or EU international students with family residing abroad must also follow the provisions of articles 30 and 31) 

The ISEE Universitario provisions in this article are addressed to students: 

1. with Italian citizenship who must present a ISEE Universitario certificate; 

2. with citizenship of a non-EU or EU country but with the family unit entirely resident in Italy 

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-02-26/96fe0d1f-109c-4be1-a3cb-bd4e5e023921/ffac2b4752cdb37cb795c2e19c65993d4546243521bb76655531e6158e3d57ce.jpg)


Non-EU or EU international students with a household partly or wholly resident abroad must submit their application in the manner indicated in arts. 30 and 31. 

Italian students who are required to submit an ISEE Parificato certificate must also submit the application by referring to the provisions of art. 6 paragraph 5.1 above. 

# Art. 7 para. 1 ACCESS CREDENTIALS AND ONLINE PROCEDURE

To submit your application, you must log on to the www.edisu.piemonte.it website. From the “ONLINE SERVICES” section, access “Scholarships, Accommodation, Catering, Refunds and Contributions” (hereinafter referred to as the Online Helpdesk) within the deadlines indicated in arts. 10 paragraph 2 (first years), 15 paragraph 2 (subsequent years), and 25 paragraph 3 (PhDs and specialisation school), with your SPID, CIE or, if you are an international student without residence in Italy, with your Temporary Access Code academic year 2025/26. 

When filling out the application, students must already be in possession of a ISEE Universitario certificate issued on or after 1 January 2025 or of the receipt attesting to the submission and signing of the DSU at the CAAF (without the relative processing of the certificate by INPS). 

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-02-26/96fe0d1f-109c-4be1-a3cb-bd4e5e023921/e33cba9a8f52d66259f58fd6cdc0761557f43d120f4ca78c7caae9cc6cf1bf0e.jpg)


When registering for its online services, EDISU Piemonte always asks you to specify an email address. It is recommended that this address be directly attributable to the requesting student, not to any other party, and that it be directly managed by them. This is because all communications, which do not fall within the scope of those that can only be viewed on their personal page of the Online Helpdesk, will be sent directly 

from the Ticketing procedure and/or information service noreply@edisu-piemonte.it (the latter address must not be used by students for communication or direct response) 

Any change in the e-mail address must be promptly communicated via the appropriate procedure available on the personal page of the Online Helpdesk. 

During the year, communications may also be sent to the student emails provided by the University. 

# Art. 7 paragraph 1.1 SPID AND CIE

Students must submit their applications by accessing the Online helpdesk procedure exclusively with SPID or CIE (Law 100/2020). 

Students in possession of the SPID or CIE must take the following steps. 

1. Fill in all the mandatory spaces of the online application. 

2. Submit your application exclusively online, by clicking on the “Submit” button, before 12:00 p.m. on the deadline day. 

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-02-26/96fe0d1f-109c-4be1-a3cb-bd4e5e023921/87eccd8eba7f7ef44f0d102c3bc16c0a580880c4f04f7df8b7705c3dad56958b.jpg)


EDISU cannot offer assistance to students accessing the procedure via SPID, who will have to apply to the body responsible for issuing it. If the problem occurs close to the deadline, open a ticket before the deadline itself, in the appropriate section of the www.edisu.piemonte.it website 

# Art. 7(1.2) TEMPORARY ACCESS CODE 2025/26

The Temporary Access Code 2025/26 is a code that is requested starting in July and expires annually (it expires in June of the following year). It can only be used by international students who do not have a SPID and cannot apply for it because they are not resident in Italy. These students must perform the following steps: 

1. Register in the Online Helpdesk to obtain the Temporary Access Code 2025/26. 

2. Fill in all the mandatory spaces of the online application for the requested benefit. 

3. Press the “FINAL SAVE” button to complete filling in. After pressing it, you will no longer be able to edit the application, so make sure that you have entered all the information requested on the previous pages that need filling in. 

4. Press the “PRINT” button: a new web tab will open in your browser where you will find the application form that must be printed on paper (except for students using the qualified electronic signature referred to in point 5 below) 

5. Sign the application form printed in accordance with point 4 above in pen and in your own hand, or with a qualified electronic (or digital) signature45. Signatures entered in word or other forms will not be accepted. 

6. Please attach only the following documents in PDF format, following the instructions in the procedure: 

a. the application form scanned and signed by the students in their own hand or with a qualified electronic signature and any authorisation form if the students are minors (art. 10(1)). 

b. black and white, double-sided copy of a valid identity document scanned on a single sheet. 

7. Submit the online application and the above-mentioned documents exclusively online, by clicking on the “SEND” button, by 12:00 p.m. on the deadline day. 

All documents must be correctly saved as .pdf and must not exceed 1 MB in size. A single PDF is required for each attachment, even if the attachment has several pages. Attachments in formats other than PDF (e.g. jpg, btm,) will not be accepted. If students attach a document that has not been correctly converted into a .pdf file, this file will be damaged and therefore not visible. Therefore, it will not be accepted for the purposes of the competition. 

Students are required to check the correctness and formats of the attached files. 

The identity document must be scanned in its entirety, both front and back, and be legible in all its parts, including the signature. Images that cannot be displayed (pixelated, blurred, distorted, incomplete, etc.) must not be attached. 

If the student accesses the application with both the SPID/CIE and the Temporary Code, they must submit it in accordance with the provisions of this paragraph for submitting the application with the Temporary Code (print, sign, attach the application, and send) 

It can take up to 6 hours from the request for the Temporary Access Code for it to be issued by EDISU. The applicant must take this into account when calculating the time needed to complete and submit the application within the deadlines set in the notice of competition, assuming full responsibility for it. 

Failure to sign the form or to present an identity document is grounds for exclusion that CANNOT be rectified with a complaint. 

Please note that access codes are strictly personal, so applications are considered to be completed directly by students holding the Temporary Access Code 2025/26. 

As this is a temporary code, students must always also attach a copy of their identity document. The temporary code 2025/26 will expire on 30 June 2026. 

Further information on the use of and application for codes can be found at www.edisu.piemonte.it. 

In the event of problems related to the loss of the Temporary Access Code or password, the wrong e-mail address or a change of e-mail address, students should use the procedures available on the Online Helpdesk login page, under “Temporary Access Code 2025/26 Assistance”. 

# Art. 7(2) RECEIPTS (CONFIRMATIONS)

Following the transmission of the application, two receipts are sent to the e-mail address indicated: 

1. The first confirmation, with the subject “Acquisizione dati via web” (acquisition of web data), is sent after the online transmission of the application. 

For students who have applied with a Temporary Access Code, the documents previously signed and attached to the application procedure are available attached. For students who have applied with a SPID, a PDF of the application form is attached and should be kept. 

2. The second confirmation, with the subject “Ricezione pratica” (receipt of file), is sent after the application has been imported into the EDISU database. The protocol number assigned to the application is indicated in the text. 

The application is deemed to have been correctly transmitted if and only if the first confirmation is delivered. Receipts will remain available on the students' personal page of the Online Helpdesk under “Ricevute” (Receipts). 

Students who entered the ISEE protocol or the DSU issuing protocol when completing the application will receive another confirmation within 48 working hours of the second confirmation with the subject “Ricevuta dati INPS” (INPS data receipt) containing the data relating to EDISU’s query of the INPS database. If EDISU does not find any valid ISEE, the reason for the lack of validity will be indicated. 

Students whose confirmation with the subject “Ricevuta dati INPS” (INPS data receipt) has the wording “In the INPS data bank there is an ISEE Certificate not valid for the right to university study for the applicant benefits” must enter the ISEE data relating to the new and corrected ISEE Universitario Certificate in the data modification procedure by 12:00 p.m. on 9 September 2025, the deadline for submitting the application. 

Students whose confirmation with the subject “Ricevuta dati INPS” (INPS data receipt) has the wording “ISEE with observations on omissions and/or discrepancies” must send the documentation proving the correctness of the contents of the DSU, as indicated in the INPS and Ministry of Labour message no. 8415 of 26/10/2020. Documentation may be submitted via the data modification procedure by 12:00 p.m. on 9 September 2025, the application deadline, or later via the ticketing system, ISEE economic requirements section. 

They may also submit a complaint, referred to in paragraph 6 below, attaching the ISEE and DSU with observations, together with the documentation proving the discrepancies found. 

Applications submitted even partially differently from those described in this article will not be accepted. The online application must be submitted by 12:00 p.m. on the deadline day. The procedure closes automatically at 12:00 p.m. on that day and the countdown is reset. After 12:00 p.m. of the deadline, it will not be possible to submit the application even if the failure to submit is due to force majeure or the fault of a third party (e.g. problems with the internet connection or the terminal being used). Any event occurring after the date on which the application is submitted (award of another scholarship or other financial aid, transfer to another university, withdrawal from studies, change of commitment from part-time to full-time and vice versa, inability to continue studies, withdrawal from enrolment, change of department or course of study, change of course venue, etc.) must be promptly communicated to the EDISU offices and documented. EDISU will check that the requirements are still met and will take any measures necessary to revoke benefits. If this isn’t the case, EDISU reserves the right to take action in relation to the failure to notify. 

# Art. 7(3) IBAN

Students must enter the SEPA IBAN via the special procedure on their personal Online Helpdesk page. 

Winners may only receive the scholarship by crediting a current account or prepaid card with an IBAN in their name or jointly in their name. Postal savings books are excluded. 

To enter an IBAN ex novo or to modify the IBAN previously entered in the EDISU database, you must access your personal page of the Online Helpdesk, fill in the procedure called “Bank Details - IBAN”, and then send the data exclusively online using the “Save and Send” button. 

Students enrolled at the University of Turin may give their consent to forward their IBAN to their University's Fees and Refunds Office in order to receive any refunds. 

After the IBAN has been communicated online, a confirmation is sent to the e-mail address indicated by the students containing the data relating to the declared code. This confirmation remains available on the students' personal page of the Online Helpdesk under “Ricevute” (Receipts). 

The scholarship will only be paid out if the IBAN has been entered within the deadlines set out in articles 13 (first years), 18 (subsequent years) and 27 (PhDs) below. 

International students, who are not allowed to open a current account under current Italian banking regulations, may enter a foreign IBAN, provided it is part of the SEPA circuit. In order to proceed with the payment, the winner must communicate an address in Italy. Until such notice, payment cannot be made. 

With regard to payments to students from certain “high-risk third countries” identified by current European legislation, delays or non-credits may occur. In this case, EDISU shall not be held liable. 

It is only possible to grant the scholarship to international students who are minors if a legal guardian is appointed, with registered residence in Italy and a current account with Italian or foreign IBAN, provided it is part of the SEPA circuit. In this case, the student who is a minor must send a copy of a notarial deed by 10 December 2025 (translated and legalised in the same way as the consular documentation referred to in art. 30(3)) in which one of the parents (or both) declares the personal data of the legal guardian and authorises payment of the scholarship to their bank account, indicating the IBAN/SEPA reference code. A copy of an identity document and the legal guardian's tax code must also be attached. 

In the absence of such a notarial deed, students who are minors must wait until they turn 18 before they can receive payment 

The sums must be collected by 31 December 2027. If the IBAN is not communicated by that date, the benefit amount is no longer payable. 

# Art. 7(4) TRANSFER OF APPLICATIONS SUBMITTED TO OTHER BODIES

Students who have applied to an Agency for the Right to Study in another region and are moving to a Piedmont University may transfer their application. To make such a transfer they must: 

• request that the institution in another region send the application to EDISU Piemonte, at the certified mail address; 

• open a ticket indicating one's personal data, tax code, telephone number, the institution where the application was submitted, as well as a front/back copy of one's ID; 

after receiving communication from EDISU Piemonte, submit the application through EDISU Piemonte’s online portal in the section "scholarship and accommodation application" within the deadlines indicated in this paragraph. 

Tranfer will be considered valid only after the transfer of the request and receipt of receipts referred to in paragraph 2 above 

The procedure described above must be completed by 22 September 2025, the deadline for submitting complaints for accommodation service (if you wish to transfer a scholarship and accommodation service application) or by 12 November 2025, the deadline for submitting complaints for the scholarship alone (if you wish to transfer a scholarship application only). 

Students who were not “non-resident” in the region where they applied for the scholarship or had not applied for the accommodation service may supplement their application by requesting the addition of the accommodation service application, if they fall under the status of “non-resident” pursuant to art. 4 and the transfer of the application takes place by 22 September 2025. 

For students who attend the "filter semester" in other regions and have submitted an application for a scholarship at that institution, there will be a re-opening of applications between 26 January and 16 February 2026 by means of the application re-opening procedure following a transfer from the Agency for the Right to Education of another region, as indicated in art. (9)(3.2) below 

# Art. 7(5) CHANGES TO THE DATA INCLUDED IN THE APPLICATION

For students who apply by logging in with a SPID or CIE, the data entered can be modified until the application is transmitted online. 

For international students applying with a Temporary Access Code academic year 2025/26, the online procedure can be relaunched in all its parts and the data entered can be modified until the “final save” button is pressed. Thereafter, the application will be frozen and it will no longer be possible to amend it; the data entered and the requests made may only and exclusively be corrected in the manner set out in section 5.1 below until 12:00 p.m. on the application deadline day. 

After the online submission of the application, the data entered can only be edited online until 12:00 p.m. on the application deadline day, for the following cases and in the following ways: 

1. Via the “DATA MODIFICATION” button, available by accessing the application for benefits from your personal Online Helpdesk page. 

a. It is possible to edit data separately for each of the following types: “Residence/domicile”, “Disability Data”, “International Protection” (only for Non-EU), “Scholastic data”, “Merit”, “Second Bachelor’s Degree Course”, “Economic Data”, “Attached Documents” (only for Temporary Access Code 2025/26). When opening each individual type, the data declared in the application are displayed in read-only mode. You only have to enter the data you wish to edit and not those you wish to confirm. Only one edit request per type can be submitted. 

b. Each edit form must be individually completed and submitted online by 12:00 p.m. on the application submission deadline day. 

2. Non-resident students who have applied for a scholarship only may add a request for accommodation service using the special “Add accommodation service application request” button, available by accessing the benefits application from their personal Online Helpdesk page. Similarly, students who have applied for a scholarship and accommodation, but only intended to apply for the scholarship may delete the request for accommodation service using the special “Delete the accommodation service application” button, available by accessing the benefits application from their personal Online Helpdesk page. 

Students who are applying for the following year for the additional semester of a Bachelor's degree but intend to enrol in a Master's degree course in the academic year 2025/26, may apply to amend the application to a first-year master’s degree one, if they meet the requirements, by editing the “Scholastic data”. 

Students enrolled in a degree course during the academic year 2022/23 who apply for the first year of a Master's degree but do not enrol, may amend their application to a subsequent-year application for the additional semester of their degree, if they have not graduated by September 2025 and if they meet the merit requirements, by editing the “Scholastic data”. 

For students with disabilities, this provision applies whether they enrolled in the academic year 2022/23 or in the academic year 2021/22. 

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-02-26/96fe0d1f-109c-4be1-a3cb-bd4e5e023921/bbe2f1faddb0043e4e723c071f36f4559ac8457f50dca858dffc8215dc10860c.jpg)


Only one data modification can be sent per type. Students are invited to check the information entered before submitting the correction. 

Requests to edit data in a manner that differs even partially from those indicated in this article will not be processed, and in any case no later than the deadline for submitting the application. 

Following online transmission, a confirmation is sent to the e-mail address indicated by the students with the subject relating to the transaction carried out (edit $^ +$ edit type, addition/deletion of accommodation), with the relevant PDF attached. 

The transaction is deemed to have been correctly transmitted if and only if this confirmation is delivered to the e-mail address the student indicates and appears in the “Ricevute” (receipts) section of their personal Online Helpdesk page. 

Sending the confirmation does not imply acceptance of the requested change: the outcome of the request will be available with the publication of the provisional ranking for the benefit requested. 

Please note that the “economic data” section of the online “data modification” procedure will be active after the transmission of the “INPS Data” receipt. 

The economic data submitted by means of the data modification procedure must refer to a ISEE Universitario certificate present in the INPS database issued even prior to the date of online retrieval, or through the submission of a new 2025 ISEE that corrects the grounds for which the EDISU did not accept it. Data edits indicating only the DSU protocol number in the absence of a processed ISEE will not be considered valid. 

Students whose confirmation with the subject “Ricevuta dati INPS” (INPS data receipt) has the wording “In the INPS data bank there is an ISEE Certificate not valid for the right to university study for the applicant benefits” must enter the ISEE data relating to the new and corrected ISEE Universitario Certificate in the Data modification procedure by 12:00 p.m., the deadline for submitting the application. 

Students whose confirmation with the subject “Ricevuta dati INPS” (INPS data receipt) has the wording “ISEE with observations on omissions and/or discrepancies” must send the documentation proving the correctness of the contents of the DSU, as indicated in the INPS and Ministry of Labour message no. 8415 of 26/10/2020. Documentation may be submitted via the Data modification procedure by 12:00 p.m. on 9 September 2025, the application deadline, or later via the ticketing system, ISEE economic requirements section. It is also possible to submit a new ISEE Universitario Certificate that rectifies the omissions/ discrepancies found in the previous one. 

After submitting the online data modification to replace the ISEE data, EDISU Piemonte does not send an additional INPS Data Receipt; therefore, the ISEE Universitario values that the student will display in the provisional rankings will be those self-certified in the modification procedure. 

They may also submit a complaint, referred to in paragraph 6 below, attaching the ISEE and DSU with observations, together with the documentation proving the discrepancies found. 

With regard to applicants for PhDs and specialisation schools, please refer to art. 25(2). 

After the application submission deadline, the data entered can only be corrected online by submitting a complaint after the publication of the provisional ranking in accordance with the procedures set out in the following paragraph. 

# Art. 7(6) COMPLAINTS AGAINST PROVISIONAL RANKINGS

Complaints may be made by both successful and unsuccessful students in the provisional ranking. Excluded students must take all grounds for exclusion into account. Only applications for the correction of material errors, relating to data found in documents dated before the application deadline, will be accepted. It is not possible to add the request referred to in paragraph 5.1, point 2 above, to a complaint. 

The complaint procedure is available by consulting the result of the provisional ranking for the benefit applied for, by selecting the “complaint” item. 

1. Separate complaints may be submitted for each of the following types: “Enrolment”, “Scholastic data”, “Merit Self-certification”, “Validations”, “Economic data”, “Pending financial obligations with EDISU” and “Other reasons” and “Second Bachelor’s Degree Course” (available only for those who have already applied for the increase by the application submission deadline). When opening each individual complaint, the data present in the provisional ranking are displayed in read-only mode. You only have to enter the data you want to edit and not the data you want to confirm. Only one complaint can be sent per type. If necessary, documents can be attached to support the complaint through the procedure, if any. You cannot rectify your exclusion with a claim based on the reason "no equal calculation" 

2. Each complaint form must be individually completed and submitted online by 12:00 p.m. on the complaint submission deadline day. 

Students who are applying for the following year for the additional semester of a Bachelor's degree but intend to enrol in a Master's degree course in the academic year 2025/26, may apply to amend the application to a first-year master’s degree one, if they meet the requirements, using a special complaint by 12 November, 12:00 p.m. 

Students enrolled in a degree course during the academic year 2022/23 who apply for the first year of a Master's degree but do not enrol, may amend their application to a subsequent-year application for the additional semester of their degree, if they have not graduated by September 2025 and if they meet the merit requirements, using a special complaint by 12 November, 12:00 p.m. 

Following the online transmission of each individual complaint, a confirmation is sent to the e-mail address indicated by the students with the subject line: “Acquisizione dati via web $^ +$ tipologia reclamo” (acquisition of web data $^ +$ complaint type). The corresponding PDF is available in the annex. 

The complaint is deemed to have been correctly sent if and only if this confirmation is delivered to the e-mail address the students indicated and appears in the “Ricevute” (receipts) section of their personal Online Helpdesk page. 

Sending the confirmation does not imply acceptance of the complaint: the outcome of the request will be available with the publication of the definitive ranking for the benefit requested. Please note that complaints must be sent by 12:00 p.m. on the deadline day. 

Please refer to arts. 12(2), (3) and (6) (first years), 17(3), (4) and (6) (subsequent years), and 26 (2), (3) and (5) (PhD and specialisation schools) for the procedures for displaying the provisional ranking and the time frame for submitting complaints. 

Complaints may not be used to put questions or doubts to EDISU. Therefore, questions posed in complaints will not be answered. The ticketing service at www.edisu.piemonte.it must be used for this purpose 

# Art. 7(6.1) COMPLAINTS AGAINST PROVISIONAL RANKINGS RELATING TO ECONOMIC DATA

Complaints against exclusions from the provisional rankings for economic reasons are compulsory in order to rectify one's position for the definitive rankings, since EDISU Piemonte will not proceed with an additional online retrieval through the INPS database before the publication of the definitive rankings. 

The economic data submitted by means of the complaint procedure must refer to an ISEE certificate present in the INPS database issued even prior to the date of online retrieval, or through the submission of a new 2025 ISEE that corrects the grounds for which the EDISU did not accept it. Complaints indicating only the DSU protocol number in the absence of a processed ISEE will not be considered valid. 

Below are the possible reasons for exclusion from the provisional ranking linked to economic reasons and indications on the possibility and method of lodging a complaint: 

• the data of the ISEE certificate or the Single Self-Declaration cannot be found in the INPS database: in this case, the data can only be rectified with a complaint if the applicant has a valid DSU for the right to university study and without observations on omissions/discrepancies signed by the deadline for the submission of the application for the benefit to be applied for; 

• the ISEE certificate is not valid for the right to University study for the benefit applicant: in this case, the data can only be rectified with a complaint if the applicant has a valid ISEE certificate for the right to university study, processed by INPS within the deadline for complaints relating to the benefit requested; 

• the ISEE certificate contains observations on omissions or discrepancies: in this case, the data can only be rectified with a complaint if the applicant has a valid ISEE certificate for the right to university study without observations on omissions/discrepancies and processed by INPS within the deadline for complaints relating to the benefit requested. 

Otherwise, the student may submit the annotated ISEE certificate with the related DSU and the documentation addressing the observations on omissions/discrepancies found46. Should students choose the latter option, EDISU Piemonte will proceed with an automatic recalculation of the ISEE certificate for internal use on the basis of the documentation submitted. The data recalculated by EDISU will be available with the publication of the definitive ranking for the benefit requested. 

If students do not send EDISU Piemonte the documentation relating to ALL the omissions/discrepancies detected in the ISEE certificate, the recalculation will NOT be carried out; 

• the ISEE certificate submitted through the Data modification procedure is not valid for participation in the competition: in this case, the data can only be rectified with a complaint in the presence of a valid ISEE certificate that can correct the type of exclusion communicated in the “INPS Data Confirmation”; 

• Incomplete and/or invalid attached documents: in this case, students are invited to check on their online helpdesk which consular documents are missing and/or invalid, and to attach the required certificates using the appropriate complaint procedure; 

• inconsistency/lack of economic documentation: in this case, students are invited to open a ticket and provide the operators with the requested information in order to clarify the applicant's economic situation. Instructions on how to submit a complaint will be provided directly to the person concerned in response to the ticket. 

# △ △

Please note that exclusion for failure to obtain the DSU by the deadline for submitting the application for benefits CANNOT be remedied with a complaint. 

In the event that students wish to submit a CURRENT ISEE, please note that the certificate must be valid on the date the complaint is submitted. 

After submitting the online complaint to replace the ISEE data, EDISU Piemonte does not send an additional INPS Data Confirmation; therefore, the ISEE Universitario values that the student will display in the definitive rankings will be those self-certified with the same procedure. 

With regard to applicants for PhDs and specialisation schools, please refer to art. 26(3). 

With regard to non-EU international students who have to submit complaints concerning consular documentation, please refer to art. 31(3). 

# Art. 7(7) WAIVER OF BENEFITS 2025/26

As of 10 September 2025, students who wish to waive a benefit must use the special “Waiver” button, available by accessing the benefit application on their personal EDISU Online Helpdesk page in “the Previous years Beneficts”. This procedure will only be activated when the application has been uploaded to the EDISU database and students receive the e-mail with the subject “Ricezione pratica” (reception of the application) (paragraphs 1.1 and 2.1 of this article). Students who have applied for both the grant and the accommodation service may renounce the accommodation service alone but cannot renounce the grant alone, since renouncing the latter necessarily entails renouncing the accommodation service. 

In the event that students are already allocated a place in EDISU residences, they must submit their renunciation directly to their University Residence reception and must fill in the online renunciation form by selecting the reason why they wish to renounce the benefit from the list within the procedure. Once completed, they must submit the request online by clicking the Send button. Students will be required to pay for the period of use in accordance with art. 35(1). 

Following the online transmission of the renunciation, a confirmation is sent to the e-mail address the students indicated with the subject line “Acquisizione dati web, rinuncia benefici 2025/26” (acquisition of web data, benefits withdrawal 2024/25). The PDF on the renunciation is available in the annex. If the student has applied for a scholarship and accommodation service, the waiver will be a "waiver of scholarship and accommodation service"; if the student has applied for a scholarship only the waiver will be a "waiver of scholarship". 

The renunciation is deemed to have been correctly sent if and only if the confirmation is delivered to the e-mail address the students indicated appears in the “Ricevute” (receips) section of their personal Online Helpdesk page. Sending the receipt does not imply automatic acceptance of the renunciation, which will be assessed and in case of refusal the applicant will be contacted. 

Renunciation entails the withdrawal of the benefits enjoyed by students and the consequent return of the monetary value thereof (art. 38). 

# Art. 8(1) NON-RESIDENT STUDENTS WHO MUST SUBMIT THE SELF-CERTIFICATION OF PAID ACCOMMODATION

Non-resident students who are not guests of EDISU residences and who belong to the categories listed in art. 5(1.3), are required to pay for accommodation, at the university location they attend (or in a neighbouring municipality), using public residential facilities or accommodation belonging to private parties or institutions for at least 10 months of the academic year 2025/26 altogether. Students must also complete the special online self-certification in accordance with the procedures and time frames set out in paragraph 2 of this article, in order to receive the non-resident amount due to them, only and exclusively if they are successful in the final scholarship rankings. Otherwise, they will be paid the amount provided for commuter students (art. 5(1.2)). 

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-02-26/96fe0d1f-109c-4be1-a3cb-bd4e5e023921/ebec098b8b2090ec7d854db1901bbca45ab6f0e6e1f9b41f4a90856d0e29e1e2.jpg)


Non-EU students with family residing abroad must also self-certify their paid residence. 

Independent students must refer to articles 5(1.3)(8) and 6(1.5) 

Students attending the “filter semester” for one of the courses pertaining to the LM-41, LM-46, LM-42 classes are also required to carefully read the provisions of art. 8(2.1) 

# Art. 8(1.1) FOREIGN/EXCHANGE STUDENTS

Those assigned a place in EDISU residences: they must follow the provisions set out in article 33(4). Students with “Erasmus Option” status with a stay abroad of less than 8 months do not have to self-certify their paid residence for the period they are away. 

2. Those who are not assigned a place in EDISU residences: they must self-certify their paid residence in the manner and time frame indicated in paragraph 2 of this article. 

In the event that the period away takes place for part of the academic year, students must submit two self-certifications, one relating to their place of residence abroad and the other to their place of residence in the municipality in which the course attended is based, so that the total period declared covers at least 10 months of the academic year 2025/26 pursuant to paragraph 1. 

# Art. 8(2) METHODS AND DEADLINES FOR SUBMITTING THE PAID ACCOMMODATION SELF-CERTIFICATION

The self-certification procedure for paid accommodation is available by accessing your personal Online Helpdesk page, during the time frames indicated in the table on the following page. When completing the form, students must indicate the duration and type of accommodation by choosing between: 

Lease contract (apartment/room): students must enter the details of their lease contract (home address, individual monthly rent not including expenses, contract identification number, date of registration with the Italian Revenue Agency, landlord's details) and attach the registration receipt issued by the Italian Revenue Agency as a .pdf file. 

It is the student's responsibility to ensure that the rental agreement: 

is duly registered with the Italian Revenue Agency: at the time of transmission of the procedure, they must have the registration confirmation issued by the Italian Revenue Agency. Otherwise, the self-certification will be considered invalid. 

• shows one's name and surname in any capacity (the contract may also be in the name of a first-degree relative, provided that he or she is not a tenant of the property. In the case of a brother/sister, the name of the scholarship applicant must also appear); in case of siblings taking over an existing contract, all tax codes must be stated on the registration receipt of the takeover. 

• is related to a property located in the municipality where the course of study attended is based, or in bordering (neighbouring) municipalities. The list of municipalities bordering the course locations is available at www.edisu.piemonte.it in the scholarship section; 

• has a duration of at least 10 months47 included in the academic year 2025/26 pursuant to paragraph 1 above 

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-02-26/96fe0d1f-109c-4be1-a3cb-bd4e5e023921/f14b97753d04de51aeb01979386f6b57eb3bd4a97cd4d8d433f77b90dfffcd9b.jpg)


You must have the contract identification number (contained in the registration confirmation issued by the Italian Revenue Agency) when completing the procedure. 

The contract registration must only be attached in the online procedure and must NOT be sent by ticket or post. 

If an existing contract is taken over, both the takeover registration receipt and the original contract registration receipt must be attached to the online procedure in a single PDF file. 

In addition, if the contract is renewed, both the original registration receipt and the renewal registration receipt must be attached, again in a single PDF file. 

The expiry date stated in the contract registration receipt or renewal receipt must be indicated in the declaration. Therefore, you cannot declare an expiry date that is not stated on a registration receipt issued by the Italian Revenue Department even in the case of contracts providing for tacit renewal. 

2. Other payment arrangement (college/boarding school/hostel/social housing): students must enter the details of the college, boarding school, or hostel they are staying at (address, tax code, individual monthly fee) for at least 10 months, in accordance with paragraph 1 above, and attach the contract (or assignment document) issued by the establishment in .pdf file Students applying for EDISU accommodation service who have selected the “Collegio Renato Einaudi” option when accepting or declaring their interest are not required to self-certify their paid residence (art. 33(5)). 

3. Foreign contract (foreign study/exchange): students must enter the details of the rental/hospitality contract and attach the contract as a .pdf file. The contract must clearly state the name of the student, the exact duration of the contract and the rental fee to be paid. For foreign/exchange students who are guests of EDISU residences, see also art. 33(4.1). Students staying at EDISU residences who have “Erasmus Option” status and stay abroad for less than 8 months do not have to submit a selfcertification of paid residence. 

Accommodation declarations made in previous academic years are not valid for the purposes of the accommodation declaration for the academic year 2025/26, even if the previously declared contract is still in force. 

Students who have submitted a declaration of paid accommodation, declaring a contract that does not cover the 10 months (including any contracts involving tacit renewals), will compete for the allocation of the commuter amount only.In any case, if funds are available, the “non-resident” amount may be supplemented on the second instalment if the paid accommodation supplementary declaration is sent, complete with the registration of the new contract or renewal of the previous one, in the period between 20 March and 12 noon on 10 April 2026. 

Contract supplements submitted after this date will not be accepted, not even by ticket. 

The self-certification must be filled in and sent exclusively online by 12:00 p.m. on the deadline day, using the “Save and Send” button. 

Following the transmission of the self-certification, a confirmation is sent to the e-mail address the students indicated with the subject line “Autocertificazione di alloggio a titolo oneroso” (Self-certification of paid accommodation). The self-certification is deemed to have been correctly sent if and only if this confirmation is received, which will remain available on the students' personal Online Helpdesk page, in the “Ricevute” (receipts) section. 

If there is a change in accommodation after the declaration has been submitted, the applicant, if a scholarship winner with a "nonresident" amount, must submit the details of the new contract. This is done through a specific online procedure: "aggiornamento contratto di locazione" relating to the contract change and the receipt of registration of the new contract must be attached to guarantee coverage of the minimum period of 10 months. This procedure will be oen fron 15 January to on 15 June 2026 at 12 noon. 

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-02-26/96fe0d1f-109c-4be1-a3cb-bd4e5e023921/c4cea66a549316a0023626d77f95dcea173f4051cfd7c468fce3eb8905130bd5.jpg)


If, during the checks, it emerges that the declared contract has been terminated without notification of a new contract or without renewal of the same (even in the case of tacit renewal), the scholarship amount will be reclassified as the amount provided for the “commuter” status. Amendment registrations made after the irregularity has been reported by EDISU will not be accepted. 

The scholarship amount is not dependent on the type of contract or the monthly rent. Therefore, the students will receive, if successful in the final scholarship rankings, the amount they are entitled to under art. 5(1.3). 

EDISU will carry out checks with the Revenue Agency to verify the actual registration of rental contracts, with the host structures in the case of a different payment basis, and spot checks on at least $30 \%$ of the declarations to ascertain the actual payment of 10 months' rent or fees. If the contract or the other payment basis is not checked, payment of the second instalment will be suspended until the check has been completed and, if necessary, the amount of the scholarship will be reduced to the “commuter” amount. 

EDISU may also require that regular payment receipts, which must be in the student's name, be submitted. Further documentation in support of the declared status may be requested: if it is not submitted by 15 June 2026, payment of the second instalment of the scholarship will be suspended. 

In addition, if checks show that the declared accommodation is not located in the municipality where the course is held or in a neighbouring municipality, the scholarship will also be reclassified as the “commuter” amount. (The list of municipalities bordering the course venues is available at www.edisu.piemonte.it). 

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-02-26/96fe0d1f-109c-4be1-a3cb-bd4e5e023921/22ad1f5a3ac099ab16d6d7c616412ce13e21a1a6f983782cfca31df4a9a6d8bf.jpg)


![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-02-26/96fe0d1f-109c-4be1-a3cb-bd4e5e023921/e41732d3870f0eed6bf6ca31031913c7e21cb99d7f5446d5a7bc643ab566ae68.jpg)
