If EDISU finds that the documentation is incomplete or erroneous, students may rectify or supplement what has been sent by submitting a formal complaint, as governed by art. 7(6.1) and art. 31(3.2) of this notice of competition. 

# Art. 30(7.1) SPECIFICATIONS FOR CONSULAR DOCUMENTATION OF INTERNATIONAL EU STUDENTS

EU international students are required to submit the consular documentation listed in section 3 above. In addition to the provisions of this paragraph, it should be noted that the consular documentation submitted by EU international students must: 

• be translated into Italian by an official translator (translations made independently will not be accepted); 

• refer only to the 2023 tax year with regard to the certification of income produced by household members; 

• refer to the date of 31 December 2023 for the certification of the real estate and movable assets of the members of the household; 

If students applying for benefits have been awarded EDISU Piemonte scholarships in previous academic years, they must submit documentation concerning the current account in their name used to receive the amounts. 

If the members of the household of EU international students reside, earn income or own property in a non-EU country, the relevant consular documentation must be issued by the authorities and legalised in accordance with the regulations in force in the country in question. 

EU international students are required to submit consular documentation using the attachment procedure available when completing the online application. For further information, see article 31(2) below. 

# INTERNATIONAL STUDENTS ENROLLED IN A PHD COURSE OR SPECIALISATION SCHOOL WHO MUST CALCULATE THE ISEE PARIFICATO

Students enrolled in a doctoral course or specialisation school who need to have their ISEE Parificato calculated can find guidance on the necessary consular documentation: 

1. in paragraph 3 above for non-EU international students; 

2. in paragraph 3 and paragraph 7 above for non-EU international students. 

# ART.31 APPLICATION PROCEDURE FOR INTERNATIONAL STUDENTS (NON-EU OR EU) WITH CONSULAR DOCUMENTATION

Non-EU students must submit consular documentation exclusively by post or courier; no other form of delivery of the abovementioned documentation will be accepted. EU students, on the other hand, will have to submit the consular documentation through the attachment procedure when filling out the online application. 

Students should therefore check the table below to find out how to submit the benefits application and consular documentation to EDISU Piemonte, and consult the following paragraphs for more information on procedures and deadlines

The online helpdesk for submission of applications can be accessed by: 



SPID or CIE: for students resident in Italy 



Temporary Access Code: for students without residence in Italy. 


# Art. 31(1) INTERNATIONAL NON-EU STUDENTS

Non-EU international students must submit benefits applications using the methods described in the following paragraphs, each of which corresponds to a step in the procedure. 

# Art. 31(1.1) OBTAINING CREDENTIALS TO ACCESS THE ONLINE APPLICATION

1. Students enrolled in the first years with an entry visa to Italy for academic year 2025/26: students in this category must calculate their tax code if they do not already have an official one. In the online registration procedure on the EDISU website, students will find information on how to calculate their tax code. After calculating the tax code, they have to register on the EDISU website by requesting a Temporary Access Code 2025/26. 

2. Students already residing in Italy but without registered residence in Italy: students belonging to this category (enrolled in both first years and subsequent years) must register on the EDISU website by requesting a Temporary Access Code 2025/26. 

3. Students already residing in Italy and with registered residence in Italy: students belonging to this category (enrolled in both first years and subsequent years) must have their SPID or CIE credentials to access the EDISU website. 

After obtaining the necessary credentials and logging in to the online counter, non-EU international students must apply online according to: 

a. the methods indicated in art. 7(1), (2) and (3); 

b. the following deadlines: 

9 September 2025 12:00 p.m. for students enrolled in the first and subsequent years of bachelor’s degree, single-cycle master’s degree, and master's degree courses (art. 10(2) and 16 (2)); 

28 November 2025 12:00 p.m. for students enrolled in the first and subsequent years of doctoral courses and specialisation schools (art. 25(2)). 

Art. 31(1.3) 

SENDING CONSULAR DOCUMENTATION TO EDISU 

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-02-26/96fe0d1f-109c-4be1-a3cb-bd4e5e023921/3b0bd675f0500c8c98fa8036649c5ae4c79ccc252ce40319145dd25624afe47a.jpg)


Students referred to in art. 30(1) do not have to submit consular documentation. For students enrolled in subsequent years who can confirm financial data submitted in previous academic years, they will have the chance to confirm their financial data within the online application procedure, in the “Financial Data” section. 

Following the transmission of the online application (art. 31(1.2)), students referred to in art. 30(2) must send the following documents to EDISU Piemonte by registered mail with return receipt or courier with proof of delivery: 

a. Consular documentation (both the original language version and the version translated into Italian) relating to the composition of the household, income and assets produced/possessed abroad by the student's household (art. 30(3) and Annex E); 

b. Copy of the Official tax code issued by the Revenue Agency or the Italian Embassy in the country of origin; 

c. For the sole purpose of file assignment, a copy of a valid ID of the student is required. The Smart Card issued by universities is not an identification document. 

d. Students who are minors must also enclose the authorisation form signed by a parent or legal guardian. The form can be downloaded from the documentation section of www.edisu.piemonte.it. 

Documentation should be sent to: 

# EDISU PIEMONTE

Via Madama Cristina 83 10126 TURIN 

The envelope must be marked with: 

1. the surname and first name of the students applying for benefits (necessarily in that order); 

2. the words 'D.C. a.a. 2025/26”. 

Consular documentation sent to EDISU Piemonte must be in original. Exceptions are marriage, divorce/legal separation or death certificates, as well as documents relating to the presence of movable assets, which may be presented as photocopies; 

EDISU Piemonte is in no way responsible for any postal or international courier delays and cannot waive the deadlines indicated in this notice of competition; 

If workers cannot match the documentation to the applicant's application record due to the absence of an identity document or the absence of surname and first name on the envelope, the file will not be assessed; 

Each student may only send their own documentation. Joint shipments of parcels containing the documentation of several students are not accepted except in cases where two or more students are sisters or brothers 

It is in no way possible to return the original documentation received in EDISU Piemonte's offices unless a formal request to renounce benefits is submitted. 

Art. 31(1.4) 

DEADLINES FOR SENDING CONSULAR DOCUMENTATION 

A) Students enrolled in the first years of a bachelor’s degree, master's degree or single-cycle master's degree: 

Documentation must be received by EDISU by 9 September 2025 to apply for the scholarship and accommodation service. If students do not deliver the documentation by 9 September 2024, they will be excluded from the provisional accommodation service rankings but will be able to re-enter the final accommodation service rankings if they deliver the required documentation by 22 September 2025. 

Documentation must be received by EDISU by 25 September 2025 to apply for the scholarship alone. If students do not deliver the documentation by 25 September 2025, they will be excluded from the provisional rankings but will be able to re-enter the final scholarship ranking if they deliver the required documentation by 12 November 2025. 

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-02-26/96fe0d1f-109c-4be1-a3cb-bd4e5e023921/3fdb033c0890622ce875b9263e5a6c6de22c2e3fdbc21770484c4946b6b63ced.jpg)


The evaluation of documentation not received by 9 September 2025 (application for scholarship and accommodation service) or 25 September 2025 (application for a scholarship only) will not be published in the provisional ranking but, if the documentation is received by the deadline for the submission of complaints, it will be published directly in the definitive ranking, without any further possibility of complaint. Therefore, students are invited to submit the required documentation in advance of the deadline to be able to have a provisional outcome and rectify any shortcomings. 

Students enrolled in a first year of a bachelor’s degree or single-cycle master’s degree who submit their documentation by 29 October 2025 at 12:00 p.m. may also be included in the final scholarship rankings of 7 November 2024 if they are duly enrolled at the University on 31 October 2025. 

If the consular documentation is still incomplete or non-compliant, students will view the negative assessment via their personal online helpdesk page and may supplement the missing/non-compliant documentation by 12 November 2025 to be included in the definitive rankings on 16 December 2025. 

# Visa delay

If students enrolled in the first year who require the accommodation service need a study visa to enter Italy for enrolment in the academic year 2025/26, they will have to declare this through the appropriate procedure when filling out the application for benefits. In the event of a delay in the visa itself and subsequent delivery of the documentation after 22 September 2025, they will be excluded from the final accommodation service ranking of 26 September 2025. However, they may be included in the definitive rankings of 16 December 2025 and in the “single scrolling ranking for accommodation service” published on 16 December 2025, in order of ISEE Parificato, if they submit all consular documentation by 12 November 2025 and enrol in the University by 30 November 2025. 

Students suspended in the rankings of 16 December 2025 who will complete registration by 3 April 2026 and will be included in the rankings of 30 April 2026, may be included in a further ranking list for the housing service which will be published on 30 April 2026. 

Students who do not complete their enrolment by 30 November 2025 may also benefit from the extension of the deadline for enrolment only at the university as set out in art. 11(2). However, the required documents must still be delivered by the deadlines indicated above. If the documentation is not received by that date, students will be definitively excluded from the definitive rankings. 

# B) Students enrolled in the subsequent years of a bachelor’s degree, master's degree or single-cycle master's degree:

Documentation must be received by EDISU by 9 September 2025 to apply for the scholarship and accommodation service. If students do not deliver the documentation by 9 September 2025, they will be excluded from the provisional accommodation service rankings but will be able to re-enter the final accommodation service rankings if they deliver the required documentation by 22 September 2025. 

Documentation must be received by EDISU by 25 September 2025 to apply for the scholarship alone. If students do not deliver the documentation by 25 September 2025, they will be excluded from the provisional rankings but will be able to re-enter the final scholarship ranking if they deliver the required documentation by 12 November 2025. 

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-02-26/96fe0d1f-109c-4be1-a3cb-bd4e5e023921/03053b5ed4da1a963f4253589e50b3d7bdb042ba4f0ec32156a288178234f105.jpg)


The evaluation of documentation not received by 9 September 2025 (application for scholarship and accommodation service) or 25 September 2025 (application for a scholarship only) will not be published in the provisional ranking. However, if the documentation is received by the deadline for the submission of complaints, it will be published directly in the definitive ranking, without any further possibility of complaint. Therefore, students are invited to submit the required documentation in advance of the deadline to be able to have a provisional outcome and rectify any shortcomings. 

# C) Students enrolled in a PhD course or specialisation school who must calculate the ISEE Parificato

EDISU must receive the documentation by 26 February 2026. If students do not deliver the documentation by 26 February 2026, they will be excluded from the provisional rankings but will be able to re-enter the definitive ranking if they deliver the required documentation by 03 April 2026. 

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-02-26/96fe0d1f-109c-4be1-a3cb-bd4e5e023921/59f2eace2462038f60b092823e2b3edda5ad3417ad22e48e6eaddfa0c8775654.jpg)


The evaluation of documentation not received by 26 February 2026 will not be published in the provisional ranking. However, if the documentation is received by the deadline for the submission of complaints, it will be published directly in the definitive ranking, without any further possibility of complaint. Therefore, students are invited to submit the required documentation in advance of the deadline to be able to have a provisional outcome and rectify any shortcomings. 

For information on the evaluation of consular documentation, please refer to paragraph 3 below. 

Please note that checks will be carried out on the presence of valid Ordinary ISEEs issued to students. 

# Art. 31(2) INTERNATIONAL EU STUDENTS

International EU students with their household residing abroad must submit their application strictly following the steps below, under penalty of exclusion from the competition. 

1. Step 1: only for those who do not have registered residence in Italy, Temporary Access Code 2025/26 request 

2. Step 2: online submission for a scholarship, or scholarship and accommodation service: The application must initially be submitted online in the manner indicated in art. 7(1), (2) and (3), by the following deadlines: 

• 9 SEPTEMBER 2025 12:00 p.m. for students enrolled in a first year or a subsequent year (including the request for an additional semester) of a bachelor's degree, master's degree or single-cycle master's degree 

• 28 NOVEMBER 2025 12:00 p.m. for students enrolled in a doctoral course or specialisation school. 

3. Step 3: submission of consular documentation via the upload procedure available when completing the online application Students must attach, via the online procedure, translated and legalised consular documentation relating to the composition, income, and assets of the student's household (art. 30 (3) and (7)) by the deadline for submitting the application for the benefit they intend to apply for. Both the documentation in the original language and the translation into Italian must be attached. 

The procedure for uploading the required documentation involves uploading a maximum of 5 attachments in .pdf version, each no larger than 1MB. Students must combine the different types of document in a single file, e.g. a single file containing the composition of the household and any divorce decrees or death certificates, another containing all the income received by the household, and one relating to movable assets (current accounts, savings, deposits, etc.) and real estate (only assessment of buildings expressed in square metres). 

The above-mentioned documentation must be enclosed with the benefits application by 9 September 2025 12:00 p.m. for students enrolled in a bachelor’s, master’s degree, or single-cycle master’s degree course. If students do not enclose the documentation by 9 September 2024, they will be excluded from the provisional rankings. However, they may be included in the definitive rankings if they deliver the required documentation by 22 September 2025 at 12:00 p.m. (application for a scholarship and accommodation service) or by 12 November 2025 at 12:00 p.m. (application for a scholarship only), attaching it to the online complaint procedure (art. 7(6) and (6.1)) 

Students enrolled in a first year of a bachelor’s degree or single-cycle master’s degree who submit their documentation by 29 October 2025 at 12:00 p.m. may also be included in the final scholarship rankings of 7 November 2025 if they are duly enrolled at the University on 31 October 2025. 

If the consular documentation is still incomplete or non-compliant, students will view the negative assessment via their personal online helpdesk page and may supplement the missing/non-compliant documentation by 12 November 2025 to be included in the definitive rankings on 16 December 2025. 

EDISU must receive the above-mentioned documentation by 28 November 2025 at 12:00 p.m. for students enrolled in doctoral courses or specialisation schools applying using the ISEE Parificato calculation. If students do not deliver the documentation by 28 November 2024, they will be excluded from the provisional rankings. However, they will be able to re-enter the definitive rankings if they deliver the required documentation by 03 April 2026 at 12:00 p.m. attaching it to the online complaint procedure (art. 7(6) and (6.1)). 

The evaluation of documentation not received by 9 September 2025 (application for those enrolled in a bachelor’s degree, master’s degree, or single-cycle master’s degree course) or 28 November 2025 (application for those enrolled in a doctoral course or specialisation school) will not be published in the provisional ranking. However, if the documentation is received by the deadline for the submission of complaints, it will be published directly in the definitive ranking, without any further possibility of complaint. Therefore, students are invited to submit the required documentation in advance of the deadline to be able to have a provisional outcome and rectify any shortcomings. 

For information on the evaluation of consular documentation, please refer to paragraph 3 below. 

Please note that checks will be carried out on the presence of valid Ordinary ISEEs issued to students. 

# Art. 31(3) ASSESSMENT AND POTENTIAL SUPPLEMENTING OF CONSULAR DOCUMENTATION OF NON-EU AND EU INTERNATIONAL STUDENTS

All consular documentation transmitted to EDISU Piemonte will be subject to evaluation based on the provisions of Article 30(3) and following paragraphs. If the certificates submitted to EDISU are assessed as invalid or incomplete, students applying for benefits will be given the opportunity to supplement the required documentation in the manner and within the time frames described in paragraph 3.2 below. 

# Art. 31(3.1) ASSESSMENT OF CONSULAR DOCUMENTATION SENT TO EDISU

The way in which the submitted documentation is assessed differs based on the nationality of the students applying for benefits (for more information, see the explanatory table at the beginning of this article). 

• CONSULAR DOCUMENTS SENT BY REGISTERED MAIL WITH RETURN RECEIPT OR COURIER WITH PROOF OF DELIVERY (NON-EU STUDENTS) 

For the acceptance of consular documentation sent by registered mail or courier, the date of arrival of the documentation at EDISU Piemonte's offices will be the valid one. 

Once the consular documentation arrives at the offices, students will receive a receipt of delivery73; the consular documentation will then be assessed by EDISU Piemonte workers and students will be able to consult the assessment at the same time as the publication of the provisional rankings on their personal Online Helpdesk page. If the certificates examined are invalid or incomplete, indications will be provided as to which documentation should be submitted. 

If the consular documentation is assessed negatively, students may send the missing/corrected documentation in accordance with the provisions of paragraph 3.2 below. 

After new documentation has been received at EDISU, the outcome will be published directly in the definitive ranking. 

The evaluation of documentation not received by 9 September 2025 (scholarship and accommodation service application for those enrolled in a bachelor’s degree, master’s degree, or single-cycle master's degree), 25 September 2025 (only scholarship application for those enrolled in a bachelor’s degree, master’s degree, or single-cycle master’s degree course), or 26 February 2026 (application for those enrolled in a doctoral course or specialisation school) will not be published in the provisional ranking. However, if the documentation is received by the deadline for the submission of complaints, it will be published directly in the definitive ranking, without any further possibility of complaint. Therefore, students are invited to submit the required documentation in advance of the deadline to be able to have a provisional outcome and rectify any shortcomings. 

Consular documentation sent to EDISU Piemonte must be in original. Exceptions are marriage, divorce/legal separation or death certificates, as well as documents relating to the presence of movable assets, which may be presented as photocopies; 

EDISU Piemonte is in no way responsible for any postal or international courier delays and cannot waive the deadlines indicated in this notice of competition; 

If workers cannot match the documentation to the applicant's application record due to the absence of an identity document or the absence of surname and first name on the envelope, the file will not be assessed; 

Each student may only send their own documentation. Joint shipments of parcels containing the documentation of several students are not accepted except in cases where two or more students are sisters or brothers 

It is in no way possible to return the original documentation received in EDISU Piemonte's offices unless a formal request to renounce benefits is submitted. 

# • CONSULAR DOCUMENTS FOR EU STUDENTS ATTACHED WHEN COMPLETING THE ONLINE BENEFITS APPLICATION

EU international students applying for benefits must submit consular documentation using the attachment procedure available when completing the online application by the application deadline for the requested benefit. 

Once the online application has been completed and sent, the consular documentation attached will be assessed by EDISU Piemonte workers and students will be able to consult the assessment at the same time as the publication of the provisional rankings on their personal Online Helpdesk page. If the certificates examined are invalid or incomplete, indications will be provided as to which documentation should be submitted. 

If the consular documentation is assessed negatively, students may send the missing/corrected documentation in accordance with the provisions of paragraph 3.2 below. 

After new documentation has been received at EDISU, the outcome will be published directly in the definitive ranking. 

The evaluation of documentation not received by 9 September 2025 at 12:00 p.m. (scholarship and accommodation service application for those enrolled in a bachelor’s degree, master’s degree, or single-cycle master's degree), 25 September 2025 at 12:00 p.m. (only scholarship application for those enrolled in a bachelor’s degree, master’s degree, or single-cycle master’s degree course), or 28 November 2025 (application for those enrolled in a doctoral course or specialisation school) will not be published in the provisional ranking. However, if the documentation is received by the deadline for the submission of complaints, it will be published directly in the definitive ranking, without any further possibility of complaint. Therefore, students are invited to submit the required documentation in advance of the deadline to be able to have a provisional outcome and rectify any shortcomings. 

# Art. 31(3.2) SUPPLEMENTING CONSULAR DOCUMENTATION ASSESSED AS INVALID OR INCOMPLETE BY EDISU PIEMONTE

For the assessment to be published in the provisional ranking, EDISU must receive the documentation by the dates indicated in the table below:

If the outcome of the documentation assessment in the definitive ranking is negative, no additional complaints can be filed and exclusion from the ranking will be final. 

Therefore, students are invited to submit the required documentation in advance of the deadline to be able to have a provisional outcome and rectify any shortcomings.

Art. 31(4) 

ADDRESSES 

FOR 

SENDING 

CONSULAR 

DOCUMENTATION 

AND 

ASSISTANCE 

Non-EU international students who need to send their consular documents by registered mail with return receipt or courier with proof of delivery should use the following address: 

EDISU PIEMONTE 

Via Madama Cristina 83 10126 TURIN 

The envelope must be marked with: 

1. the surname and first name of the students applying for benefits (necessarily in that order); 

2. the words 'D.C. a.a. 2025/26”. 

We recommend sending by registered letter with return receipt or courier with proof of delivery. For compliance with deadlines, the date of arrival at EDISU Piemonte's offices is the valid one. 

The ticketing system is the main tool for communicating with EDISU Piemonte's offices and receiving assistance. 

More information is available on the institutional website www.edisu.piemonte.it 

# Art. 31(5) CAREER SHORTENING

International students who obtain a career shortening74, due to recognition of credits relating to qualifications obtained or examinations taken at a foreign University, must refer to the articles: 

9(2), if they are enrolled in a first year and apply for the career shortening in 2025/26; 

2. 15(5), if they are already enrolled in a year subsequent to the first and have applied for a career shortening in academic years prior to 2025/26 or are applying for it in the academic year 2025/26. 

For students changing course type from a bachelor’s degree or single-cycle master's degree to a master’s degree and vice versa, the year of enrolment at the previous level is not taken into account for the purposes of the scholarship. These students will have to submit new consular documentation. 

# Art. 31(6) CHANGES TO DATA SENT VIA WEB

International students may edit the data declared in the application in accordance with the procedures and time frames indicated in art. 7(5) and (6). 

With regard to amending or supplementing consular documentation, please refer to paragraph 3 above. 

# Art. 31(7) CHANGES TO THE APPLICATION

International students may edit their applications in accordance with the procedures and time frames set out in the articles 

1. paragraph 3 above, for amendments or supplements to the consular documentation sent to EDISU Piemonte; 

2. 7(5), for changes to the data entered in the application by the submission deadline; 

3. 7(6), for the submission of complaints after the provisional rankings; 

# Art. 31(8) RENOUNCING BENEFITS 2025/26

International students may renounce the benefits applied for in accordance with the procedures and time frames indicated in art. 7(7). 

# Art. 31(9) ACCEPTANCE OF ACCOMMODATION SERVICE

International students must accept the accommodation they have won or been allocated online in accordance with the procedures and time frames set out in the following art. 33, for those who have applied as a first-year or subsequent-year student in a bachelor’s degree, master's degree, or single-cycle master’s degree 

There is no accommodation service application for doctoral and specialisation school courses 

# Art. 31(10) ASSIGNMENT OF ACCOMMODATION SERVICE

The procedures for assignment and transfer of residence are set out in art. 34. 

# Art. 31(11) NON-RESIDENT STATUS

# International students

1. with a household residing abroad (in an EU or non-EU country); 

2. with a household residing in Italy, in a municipality classified as being outside the municipality where the course attended is located (art. 4). The household is considered to be in Italy even if only one member, in addition to the student, resides in Italy and generates income. 

Are considered as non-resident only if they self-certify their paid residence in accordance with the procedures and time frames identified in art. 8(2). Otherwise, if they are awarded a grant, they will be paid the amount provided for commuter students (art. 5(1.2)). 

# Art. 31(12) VERIFICATION OF MERIT AND WITHDRAWAL OF BENEFIT

International students are subject to merit checks and possible withdrawal of the benefits in accordance with the procedures and time frames set out in arts. 13(10) and (47).

# ART. 33 ACCEPTANCE OF THE ACCOMMODATION SERVICE

Upon publication of the final accommodation service rankings, the list of available spots for each university residence in the Turin, Alessandria, Cuneo, Novara, and Vercelli campuses is published on the EDISU website, divided by: 

first-year students of a bachelor’s degree and single-cycle master's degree, divided into Italian/EU residents and non-EU students with family residing in a non-EU country; 

2. subsequent-year students and the first-year students of a master's degree. 

Students who have been successful in the final accommodation service ranking must proceed to “acceptance”. Those who are eligible in the final accommodation service ranking must proceed to “expression of interest” by filling in the online procedures that will be activated at the same time, according to the procedures and within the deadlines indicated in paragraphs 1 and 2 of this article. Students enrolled in doctoral courses or specialisation schools, on the other hand, must refer to the provisions set out in art. 28. 

In the following days, students will receive an e-mail from noreply@EDISU-piemonte.it with the details of the assignment, indicating the destination residence and entry period in accordance with the provisions of art. 34 below. 

Students who refuse a place on acceptance or expression of interest or do not complete and submit the above online procedures will be considered “commuter” students for the purposes of the scholarship amount. 

To compete for the amount provided for non-resident students, students who apply for the accommodation service but are no longer interested in a spot may: 

• delete the accommodation service request by 12:00 p.m. on 9 September 2025 by clicking on “delete accommodation”; 

submit an “accommodation service renunciation” by 12:00 p.m. on 22 September 2025, by means of a complaint against the provisional accommodation service ranking; 

They must also complete and send the self-certification of paid accommodation in the manner and within the time limits set forth in art. 8(2) and in accordance with art. 5(1.3). If students do not submit this self-certification, the amount of the grant will be equivalent to the grant for commuter students. 

Students who enter the residence and subsequently give up their allocated accommodation must repay the value of the accommodation service used, calculated at €8.18 per day. 

Students who have been awarded scholarships and are eligible for the accommodation service because they attend course venues that do not have EDISU residences do not have to accept online (paragraph 1 of this article) or declare their interest (paragraph 2 of this article). To receive the grant amount inclusive of the monetised value of the unused accommodation spot (art. 5(1.3)), they must self-certify their paid accommodation, in accordance with the methods and time frames indicated in art. 8(2). 

# Art. 33(1) WINNERS: ONLINE ACCEPTANCE

Successful students in the final accommodation service ranking must accept the spot by means of the special “Acceptance” procedure, available by accessing the accommodation service ranking from their personal EDISU Online Helpdesk page. Acceptance must be completed and submitted exclusively online according to the time frames indicated in the following table: 

<table><tr><td>Student type</td><td>Online acceptance</td></tr><tr><td>EU and non-EU accommodation winners at course locations with EDISU residences</td><td>From 26 to 30 September 2025 12:00 p.m.</td></tr></table>

They must select one of the following options when completing the acceptance: 

accepted; 

2. I accept: “I declare that I am participating in a foreign study/exchange programme of less than 8 months” (Erasmus Month Option para.4.1) or “I declare that I am participating in a foreign study/exchange programme of 8 months or more” (Erasmus Year Option – para. 4.2 of this article); 

3. I accept with “Renato Einaudi Option” (paragraph 5 of this article); 

4. I refuse. 

When accepting online, students should put all available EDISU residences in order of preference in the procedure. 

In the case of the “Erasmus Month Option”, the period of stay abroad must be indicated, specifying the dates of departure and return, which, for the sole purpose of supplementing the grant amount, must be between 1 October 2025 and 30 September 2026. The period before 1 October 2025 and after 30 September 2026 cannot be considered for these purposes. Please note that the stay abroad cannot relate to a travel/exchange project for the academic year 2026/27. 

In the case of the “Renato Einaudi Option” (see art. 33(5)), the list of EDISU residences for expressing one's preference will not be present in the procedure as the student cannot be accommodated in any residence in accordance with art. 33(4.1) and (5). 

You must also complete all additional fields in the procedure if they are not already pre-filled (personal data, residence permit or residence permit application receipt) and read and accept the relevant information required for the subsequent allocation of the accommodation. 

The online acceptance is considered to be correctly completed and transmitted if and only if confirmation (receipt) is sent to the students' e-mail address with the PDF of the completed form attached. The receipt is also available on your personal EDISU Online Helpdesk page, in the “Ricevute” (receipts) section. 

Only one confirmation (receipt) will be sent. Should students, upon checking their confirmation, verify that they have made mistakes in completing the procedure, they may complete ONE online data change within the Acceptance submission deadline. 

Failure to complete and transmit the online acceptance by 12:00 p.m. on the deadline day is equivalent to a refusal of the accommodation service. 

Students who refuse a place on acceptance or do not submit the procedure online will be considered “commuter” students for the purposes of the scholarship and will not be able to submit the declaration of paid accommodation 

At their request, however, they may be placed at the bottom of the sliding list to be accommodated in a residence free of charge. These students will not be able to make the paid residence declaration 

Eligible students in the final accommodation service ranking must declare their interest in obtaining a place in EDISU residences by filling in and transmitting the special procedure, called “Expression of Interest”, online. This is available by accessing the accommodation service ranking from their personal Online Helpdesk page, according to the time frames indicated in the following table: 

<table><tr><td>Student type</td><td>Expression of Interest</td></tr><tr><td>Those eligible for EU and non-EU accommodation at course locations with EDISU residences</td><td>From 26 to 30 September 2025 12:00 p.m.</td></tr></table>

They must select one of the following options when completing the expression of interest: 

1. I am interested. 

2. I am interested “I declare that I am participating in a foreign study/exchange programme of less than 8 months” (Erasmus Month Option para. 4.1) or “I declare that I am participating in a foreign study/exchange programme of 8 months or more” (Erasmus Year Option – para. 4.2 e of this article); 

3. I am interested with “Renato Einaudi Option” (paragraph 5 of this article); 

4. I am not interested. 

Students who declare that they are interested must express their order of preference for all available EDISU residences in the procedure. If spots are available, they will be allocated accommodation in the residences still available after acceptance of the winning students. 

In the case of the “Erasmus Option”, the period of stay abroad must be indicated, specifying the dates of departure and return, which, for the sole purpose of supplementing the grant amount, must be between 1 October 2025 and 30 September 2026. The period before 1 October 2025 and after 30 September 2026 cannot be considered for these purposes. Please note that the stay abroad cannot relate to a travel/exchange project for the academic year 2026/27. 

Before online submission, students must also complete all additional fields in the procedure if they are not already pre-filled (personal data, residence permit or residence permit application receipt) and read and accept the relevant information required for the subsequent allocation of the accommodation. 

For the “Erasmus Option” please refer to the University guidelines for students’ foreign study/exchange in the first semester of the academic year 2025/26, which define the remote start of student foreign study/exchange, the relevant scholarship disbursement methods, and the further postponement of the start of the foreign study/exchange. These guidelines will also be taken into account for accepting the accommodation and the availability of the accommodation given to students. 

They will have to submit the paid accommodation declaration by the deadline and in the manner laid down in art. 8 above to compete for the scholarship with a non-resident amount. 

The expression of interest is considered to be correctly completed and transmitted if and only if confirmation (receipt) is sent to the students' e-mail address with the PDF of the completed form attached. The receipt is also available on your personal EDISU Online Helpdesk page, in the “Ricevute” (receipts) section. 

Only one confirmation (receipt) will be sent. Should students, upon checking their confirmation, verify that they have made mistakes in completing the procedure, they may complete ONE online data change within the Expression of Interest. 

Failure to complete and transmit the expression of interest procedure online by 12:00 p.m. on the deadline day is equivalent to having selected the “I am not interested” option. 

Once the expression of interest is closed, the Outcome of the declarations of interest is published on 2 October 2025, available by accessing the accommodation service ranking from your personal EDISU Online Helpdesk page. 

Depending on the option chosen in the expression of interest, and whether or not students were “allocated” accommodation, the possible results of the allocation are as follows: 

If students have declared “I am interested”, or “I am interested with Erasmus Option” and have been allocated accommodation, EDISU will send an e-mail to students with details of the allocation from the procedure (noreply@EDISU-piemonte.it) in the following days. If they give up their place after checking in, they will compete for the scholarship for the commuting amount only. 

1. If students have declared “I am interested”, or “I am interested with the Erasmus Option” but it turns out that they have NOT been allocated accommodation, they are included in the single scrolling rankings (paragraph 3 of this article) and compete for the amount of the scholarship including the monetised value of the unused accommodation service (art. 5(1.3) point a), should they be scholarship winners and submit the declaration of paid accommodation; 

2. If students have declared “I am interested with the Renato Einaudi Option” they must follow the provisions set out in paragraph 5 of this article. 

The outcome for first-year students is broken down by course level and indicated therein: 

1. the position of students; 

2. the option chosen by the students in the expression of interest; 

3. the allocation or non-allocation of accommodation. For students who have declared “I am interested” or “I am interested with the Erasmus Month” Option, the allocation of accommodation can take place at course type or University level. Initially, the spots remaining after the winners’ acceptance are redistributed to eligible students of the same course level. Any spots still left over are redistributed within the University and, finally, if there are additional seats to be allocated, a final distribution is made based on the course location only. 

The outcome for subsequent-year students is broken down by department and indicated therein: 

1. the position of students; 

2. the option chosen by the students in the expression of interest; 

3. the result of the allocation. For students who have declared “I am interested” or “I am interested with the Erasmus Month” Option, the allocation can take place at the department, course type, or University level. Initially, the spots remaining after the acceptance of the winners are redistributed to eligible students of the same department. After this distribution, any places left over are redistributed among all departments at the same course level among the students still to be allocated. Any spots still left over are redistributed within the University and, finally, if there are additional seats to be allocated, a final distribution is made based on the course location only. 

# Art. 33(3) ELIGIBLE: SINGLE SCROLLING RANKINGS

At the same time as the publication of the expression of interest Outcomes, on 2 October 2025, new rankings will be published for eligible students who declared an interest but were not allocated accommodation in the expression of interest outcomes. These rankings are referred to as “Single Scrolling Rankings” and are drawn up as follows: 

1. for the first years, divided between EU/Non-EU students and course location, then ordered by increasing ISEE Universitario (or ISEE Parificato); 

2. for subsequent years, divided by course location, then ordered by decreasing score. 

If their score is equal, students with a lower ISEE Universitario have priority. If the ISEE Universitario is the same, younger students have priority. The single scrolling rankings can be consulted by accessing the accommodation service ranking from the personal EDISU Online Helpdesk page. 

For more information on updating your ranking, please write to assegnazioniresidenze@edisu-piemonte.it. 

If accommodation becomes available, the Accommodation Service Department will contact the students in order of ranking in order to allocate it, in accordance with the allocation criteria that will be published prior to the accommodation acceptance period. Students will receive an e-mail from assegnazioniresidenze@edisu-piemonte.it to the e-mail address they indicated in their application. The sliding procedures will close on 30/04/2026. 

For those who have been allocated accommodation using the scrolling ranking, the scholarship amounts vary as follows. 

# Art. 33(3.1) STUDENTS ACCEPTING ACCOMMODATION ALLOCATED BY SCROLLING RANKING

In the case of winners in the final scholarship rankings: 

1. If the accommodation service is accepted before the publication of the final grant rankings (16 December 2025), the value of the accommodation service calculated at € 245.45 per month (the month is counted if students enter the residence up to the 15th day of the month) will be deducted from the grant amount including the monetised value of the accommodation (art. 5(1.3)). 

2. If the accommodation service is accepted after the publication of the final grant rankings (16 December 2025): if students have self-certified the cost of accommodation (art. 8(2)), the deduction relating to the value of the accommodation service actually used will be made from the second grant instalment; if students have not self-certified the cost of accommodation, they will receive the commuter grant amount (art. 5(1.2)) but are still entitled to use the accommodation free of charge. 

If allocated the accommodation service, eligible students in the final grant rankings are entitled to free accommodation (art. 5). Eligible students in the final scholarship rankings who lose the right to their allocated accommodation will have to repay the value of the accommodation service used. 

Inclusion in the single scrolling ranking does not necessarily imply the allocation of accommodation during the academic year, as it is subject to the availability of accommodation. In December 2025, the scrolling rankings will be suspended to allow the final scholarship rankings to be drawn up until they are published. 

# Art. 33(3.2) STUDENTS REFUSING ACCOMMODATION ALLOCATED BY SCROLLING RANKING

In case of winners in the final scholarship rankings: 

1. If students have self-certified their paid accommodation (art. 8), then they receive the grant amount including the monetised value of the unused accommodation (art. 5(1.3)). 

2. If students have not self-certified their paid accommodation, they receive the commuter grant amount (art. 5(1.2)). 

Eligible applicants in the final grant rankings are not entitled to receive any monetisation of the accommodation service. 

Students who in the academic year 2025/26 participate in foreign study/exchange programmes of their Universities or AFAM must select the option “Erasmus Month” (to participate in a foreign study/exchange programme of less than 8 months) or “Erasmus Year” (to participate in a foreign study/exchange programme of 8 months or more) when accepting or expressing their interest. 

# Art. 33(4.1) Erasmus Month Option

Students who win or are eligible for the accommodation service at an EDISU residence and who spend a period abroad of less than 8 months as part of a foreign study/exchange programme must accept the place with the “Erasmus Month” Option. 

Students applying for the accommodation service as “last semester” students must submit their acceptance (successful) or expression of interest (eligible) with Erasmus month option, regardless of the duration of the period abroad 

During acceptance (successful) or expression of interest (eligible), students must indicate the precise period of their stay abroad, starting on 1 October 2025. 

In the case of the Option, I declare that “I am participating in a foreign study/exchange programme of less than 8 months” the period of stay abroad must be indicated. The student specifies the dates of departure and return, which, for the sole purpose of supplementing the grant amount, must be between 1 October 2025 and 30 September 2026. The period before 1 October 2025 and after 30 September 2026 cannot be considered for these purposes. Please note that the stay abroad cannot relate to a travel/exchange project for the academic year 2026/27. 

After acceptance, and no later than 10 October 2025, students must submit the following via the ticketing procedure as a registered student: 

a. a copy of the document, issued by their university's foreign study/exchange office, showing the details of the study/exchange project; 

Should the accommodation be allocated during the academic year, this documentation must be submitted at the time of acceptance. 

In addition, these students: 

1. do not have to self-certify their paid accommodation; 

2. must notify their residence of their departure and return dates at least 10 days in advance: otherwise, the availability of the place on return will not be guaranteed; 

3. only if they are awarded a grant, receive a total amount supplemented with the monetised value of the unused accommodation of € 245.45 per month (the month is only counted if students leave the residence by day 15 or return to the residence by day 16). 

Guests of an EDISU residence who win a foreign study/exchange project after acceptance, during the academic year, must promptly submit their application via the ticketing procedure as a registered student: 

your personal details, the residence to which you have been assigned, and the type of foreign study/exchange project in which you are participating must be indicated in the text; 

2. the following must be attached: 

a. a copy of the document, issued by their university's foreign study/exchange office, showing the details of the study/exchange project; 

No supplements of the grant amount will be made for projects in the academic years 2024/25 and 2026/27 or for periods communicated to EDISU after 15 June 2026. 

The same provisions concerning foreign study/exchange may also be applied in cases of Theses or Internships planned by the University in locations other than those of the University. 

# Art. 33(4.2) Erasmus Year Option

Students who are awarded the accommodation service at an EDISU residence and who spend a period abroad of more than 8 months as part of a foreign study/exchange programme must accept the place with the “Erasmus Year” Option. 

Subsequently, these students must self-certify their paid accommodation in accordance with the procedures and time frames indicated in art. 8(2): in this case, only if they are successful in the final grant rankings, they will receive a total amount supplemented with the monetised value of the unused accommodation (art. 5(1.2)). 

If they return early, the Accommodation Service sector will assess the possible request for the allocation of a free place in the EDISU residences, based on the availability of places. For the purposes of the second grant instalment, the student will be considered an “Erasmus Month” instead of an “Erasmus Year” student and a deduction of € 245.45 will be made from the second scholarship instalment for each month of early return 

In addition to submitting the document from the University certifying the extension of the period, students participating in exchange/study projects as Erasmus Month students who, following extensions of the period fall into the “Erasmus Year” category, must also submit the contract certifying their paid accommodation for the entire period of away by sending the above-mentioned documentation by ticket. 

# Art. 33(5) GUESTS OF THE RENATO EINAUDI COLLEGE: RENATO EINAUDI OPTION

Students who have won a place at the Renato Einaudi College for 2025/26 and are enrolled in the first or subsequent years must accept the EDISU place (if successful) or express their interest (if eligible) with the Renato Einaudi Option. In addition, these students: 

1. do not have to self-certify their paid accommodation; 

2. only if they are grant winners, they receive a total amount supplemented with the monetised value of the EDISU place not used (art. 5(1.3)). 

Guest students at the Renato Einaudi College with an INPS grant o or other scholarships type of accommodation service scholarship are not eligible for this option. 

# ART. 34 ALLOCATION OF ACCOMMODATION AT EDISU RESIDENCES

Accommodation allocation consists of the right to use one of the places on offer at university residences located in the region. Allocation does not amount to a student's choice of the type of accommodation but consists solely of the right to use the service. 

# Art. 34(1) ALLOCATION CRITERIA

Residencies are allocated in the following order of priority: 

• For confirmations by merit in subsequent years and for winners by standard application in subsequent years, the accommodation is allocated based on a single ranking drawn up solely in order of points, taking into account the order of preference expressed at the time of acceptance; 

• For confirmations by merit in the first year of a master’s degree, the accommodation is allocated on the basis of a single ranking in order of ISEE Universitario/Parificato, taking into account the order of preference expressed at the time of acceptance; 

• For first-year bachelor’s, master's, and single-cycle master’s degree winners by standard application, divided between EU and non-EU students, the accommodation will be allocated based on a single ranking in order of ISEE Universitario/Parificato, taking into account the order of preference expressed at the time of acceptance. 

If students occupy the same position in the ranking, preference is given to those already allocated a place in 2024/25. 

After the winners’ allocation, the allocation relating to eligible candidates, who are assigned accommodation in the expression of interest, is carried out in the same way as for the winners. 

The allocation criteria are published under Housing $>$ Competitive Accommodation Service on the EDISU website. 

Students winners of the final rankings of 26 September who refuse the allocation, or do not turn up at the residence on the dates indicated in the allocation e-mail at the time of allocation, will be considered “commuter” students for the purposes of the scholarship amount (art. 5(1.2)). 

# NOVITÀ

Students who are eligible in the final accommodation service ranking but state that they are not interested in the interest declaration step or do not submit the interest declaration procedure art. 33(2) or give up the place attributed in the “interest declaration outcomes” step (give up the place when the residence is assigned or fail to turn up at the assigned residence on time) can compete for the scholarship amount as a non-resident, by submitting the paid housing declaration in the manner and by the deadline set out in art. 8. If, on the other hand, they give up their place after checking in, they can no longer submit the paid accommodation declaration and only contribute to the commuter scholarship amount. 

Justified extensions may be requested on entry to the Residence. The request for an extension of the entry into a residence must be submitted by sending the extension form available on the website to assegnazioniresidenze@edisu-piemonte.it. 

The request for an extension will be considered as an acceptance of the allocation, starting from the last day for entry into the Residence. Therefore, if students do not present themselves at the residence at the end of the extension period, they will be deemed to have withdrawn and will have to pay the value of the accommodation service, calculated at $\notin 8 . 1 8$ per day, for the period for which they have requested the extension. 

Should students requesting an extension renounce during the course of the year, they will have to pay the value of the accommodation service, calculated at $\notin 8 . 1 8$ per day, from the allocation in residence, and not from the check-in date. 

Students who have requested an entry extension have the accommodation kept for them until 31 December 2025 exclusively for the following situations: 

Students enrolled in master's degree courses for the academic year 2025/26 awaiting a bachelor's degree at non-Piedmont Universities or at a university city in Piedmont other than the city of residence of the allocation; 

2. Students with documented health problems that prevent them from entering within the time limit set out in the allocation email; 

3. Students who document their participation in training activities (courses, internships, placements, etc.) in a city other than the city of residence of the allocation; 

4. International first-year students who are unable to arrive in Italy by the date of allocation of residence (art. 31). 

Even if the accommodation is kept available until 31 December 2025, the amount deducted from the scholarship will be counted from the last day provided in the allocation email and not from check-in. 

Students applying for a first-year of a bachelor’s or master’s degree for the Turin/Grugliasco site will only be housed in the Borsellino, Cappel Verde, Cavour, Claretta, Olimpia, Mollino, Codegone, Cstudio, Sanpaolo, Campus x, Moi, Liborio, Lingotto, Paoli and Verdi residences and for the Novara site in the Castalia residence, as they are equipped with a security service. 

Students participating in foreign study/exchange projects will be accommodated at the facilities indicated by the allocation criteria that will be published prior to the accommodation acceptance period. 

# Art. 34(1.1) ROOM TYPE

The room type (single, double, triple) is allocated based on academic seniority, in order of ranking, subject to available places, and according to the allocation criteria that will be published prior to the period of accommodation acceptance, which will take into account suitable accommodation solutions for students with special documented needs or over 30 years of age. 

Single rooms that become vacant during the year, following the attainment of qualifications or renunciation/withdrawal of the accommodation service, will be allocated firstly to students already in the residence in order of academic seniority and ranking, upon request, then to eligible students not called up. 

# Art. 34(1.2) TRANSFERS FOR HEALTH OR PERSONAL SAFETY REASONS

Students can request transfer to another residence for documented health reasons or for personal safety, which EDISU reserves the right to assess, according to the allocation criteria that will be published prior to the period of accommodation acceptance. 

Students enrolled in the first year of a master’s degree and subsequent years may request a transfer to any residence, while those enrolled in a first year of a bachelor's degree or single-cycle master's degree may only request a transfer to another residence with a security service. 

# Art. 34(1.3) MOBILITY BETWEEN DIFFERENT RESIDENCES

Transfers between residences will be permitted throughout the academic year. Such swaps take place during the periods (mobility windows) indicated in the relevant calendar and in accordance with the procedures set out in the relevant regulations, which will be made known as of 1 October 2025 by publication on the website www.edisu.piemonte.it 

Users interested in the periods (mobility windows) indicated in the relevant calendar will be able to make the request via their personal profile on the online portal. 

# Art. 34(2) ALLOCATION PROCEDURE

Students who have accepted accommodation will receive an e-mail from noreply@EDISU-piemonte.it with details of the allocation. Students must present themselves at the residence for allocation by the deadline indicated in the e-mail provided with: 

1. a valid identity document (for non-EU students, the identity document must be a passport); 

2. residence permit (or copy of the receipt of payment for the residence permit) for non-EU students; 

3. passport photo; 

4. copy of registration with the National Health Service (health card) or copy of a private insurance policy for non-EU students76. 

# Art. 34(3) RULES FOR ASSIGNEES

By accepting the place, students undertake to comply with the provisions of this notice and the Internal Regulations for University Residences. The following rules shall also be applied: 

Students will not be granted accommodation if they have not paid their outstanding fees of any kind for the previous academic years (EDISU has the right to take action to recover these sums) or if they have incurred a revocation of their benefits as provided for in the internal residence regulations. 

2. Students may not enter the residence until they have completed the procedure relating to the acceptance and allocation of the accommodation and handed in the documentation indicated in paragraph 2 of this article, and in any case no later than 48 hours after the deadline for allocation. 

3. The accommodation is reserved exclusively for students, who may not cede its use, even temporarily, to others, under penalty of forfeiture of benefits. 

4. Security provisions: 

a. During their year of residence, accommodation assignees must participate in at least one of the evacuation drills organised in their allotted residence; 

b. It will be mandatory to attend information and training meetings organised by EDISU related to security. The calendar will be announced after the date of entry into the residence. 

Disciplinary proceedings will be initiated against them in the event of failure to participate in what is indicated in points a and b. 

Full provisions on residence accommodation and related sanctions can be found in the “Internal Regulations for University Residences”, which can be found in the “Housing” section of www.edisu.piemonte.it and at the reception desk of one’s residence. 

<table><tr><td>Student type</td><td>Allocation period</td></tr><tr><td>First and subsequent years</td><td>6 October 2025 to 25 September 2026</td></tr><tr><td>additional semester</td><td>6 October 2025 to 31 March 2026</td></tr></table>

# Art. 34(5) SUMMER CLOSURE

The residences will be closed during the summer period from 24 July to 1 September 2026 and during periods not included in the table in paragraph 4 of this article. 

Some residences will remain open in August 2025 for students who need to stay as guests during the summer period: interested parties must indicate this need when accepting their place. Requests received after acceptance will be assessed by the Accommodation Service sector based on the availability of places. 

Students staying in residence during the month of August will be required to pay the fee of $\notin 8 . 1 8$ per day for a minimum of 7 consecutive nights (in the period from 4 August to 29 August, students will be required to pay a minimum of 7 nights even for shorter stays). 

Changes to the summer residence application must be received by 4 August via the ticketing service 

Payment for the summer residence must be made in advance when entering the Residence, as stipulated 

by the Internal Regulations for Residences. This rule is also applied to students already in the summer residence facilities. 

# Art. 34(6) SPECIAL CASES

Should a student who, for documented health reasons, pregnancy, or dependent children, be unable to live in an EDISU residence, they may be eligible for the scholarship amount including the value of the accommodation service if they certify paid residence in accordance with the procedures and within the deadlines laid down in art. 8(2) above. The student will still have to complete the online acceptance procedure (if a winner) or expression of interest (if eligible) and declare their status via a ticket. The same provisions apply to the cases indicated in art. 29(5). 

# Art. 34(6.1) ADDITIONAL SEMESTERS

1. Students receiving the accommodation service for an additional semester who graduate by 31 March 2026 must: 

a. Promptly notify their residence of the date of graduation, as soon as it is known, and leave the residence within 10 days of that date. 

b. If the degree is awarded after 31 March 2026, but according to the course schedule falls within the March graduation session, students must promptly notify their residence and the accommodation service office through the ticketing procedure of the expected graduation date or graduation period. They should bear in mind that they must also notify their residence of the date of graduation and vacate the accommodation within 10 days of that date. 

c. Otherwise, students will have to repay an amount equal to the value of the accommodation service unduly used, in the period between the eleventh day after the date of graduation and the date of check-out from the residence, at the residence rate. 

d. The value of the accommodation service in the period between the date of removal from the residence and 31 March 2026 will not be reimbursed in any way. 

Leaving before 31 March 2026 does not constitute a renouncement for students benefiting from the accommodation service for an additional semester. They will not have to pay for the period used. 

# Art. 34(6.2) STUDENTS WITH “SUSPENDED” OUTCOME IN THE DEFINITIVE SCHOLARSHIP RANKING OF 16 DECEMBER 2025

They can remain in residence until the publication of the definitive scholarship rankings on 30 April 2026. 

1. Students who apply for a first year of a master's degree and are assigned the accommodation service but do not enrol in a master's degree course by 3 April 2026: 

• if they qualify for being considered in their last semester of the degree, they will have to leave the residence and pay for the period used from 1 April 2026 

if they qualify for being considered in their last semester of the degree, they will have to leave the residence and pay for the whole period used starting from the allocation date. 

2. Students who apply as subsequent-year students and are assigned the accommodation service, but do not complete their enrolment or are not awarded the credits set forth in Table A2 by 3 April 2026, will have to leave their residence within 3 working days and pay for the entire period used from the allocation date. 

# Art. 34(6.3) STUDENTS WHO MUST LEAVE THEIR RESIDENCE FOR SERIOUS REASONS

Students who have to leave their residence during the academic year due to natural disasters or particularly serious reasons, concerning the students themselves or their family members that are adequately documented/certified, do not have to return any amount equal to the value of the accommodation used. 

These students can return free of charge in September if they are enrolled in the first year of a master’s degree in the academic year. 2026/27. If they do not enrol, they will have to pay for the month of September at student residence fees. 

# ART. 35 REVOCATION OF ACCOMMODATION SERVICE DUE TO RENUNCIATION OR LOSS OF REQUIREMENTS

# Art. 35(1) REVOCATION FOR WAIVER OF ACCOMMODATION SERVICE 2025/26

Please note that, as stipulated in art. 5(1.2), if students give up their place at the time of allocation or after entering the residence (check-in) for the purposes of the scholarship amount, they are demoted to “commuters”. 

Students who enter the residence and subsequently give up their allocated accommodation must repay the value of the accommodation service used, calculated at €8.18 per day. 

# Art. 35(2) WITHDRAWAL OF THE ACCOMMODATION SERVICE DUE TO LOSS OF REQUIREMENTS

The cases of withdrawal of the allocated accommodation service and payment for the period used are set out in the following articles of this notice. 

# 1. First years (Section III)

a. Students enrolled in the first year of courses who do not achieve merit for the maintenance of the first instalment of the scholarship, in accordance with the provisions of art. 13(5) “Specific provisions for winners assigned a place at an EDISU residence”. 

b. Eligible students in the definitive scholarship rankings who do not meet the merit requirements, in accordance with the provisions of art. 13(6.1) “Specific provisions for eligible students assigned a place at an EDISU residence”. 

c. Students who apply as a first-year student of a master's degree, request both the grant and the accommodation service, but do not enrol in a master's degree course by 3 April 2026: 

• with requirements for the additional semester of a degree will have to pay for the period used from 1 April 2025 

• without requirements for the additional semester of a degree will have to pay for the period used from the checkin date 

d. Students excluded from the provisional scholarship rankings who do not intend to lodge a complaint, in accordance with art. 12(2) “Provisional rankings”. 

e. Students excluded from the definitive accommodation service and scholarship rankings, in accordance with art. 12(4) and (5) “Definitive rankings”. 

f. Students whose benefits have been withdrawn following a financial or merit assessment, including for previous academic years. 

g. Students whose benefits have been withdrawn because of an offence committed in the Residence in accordance with the Internal Regulations for Residences. 

# 2. Subsequent years, additional semesters (Section IV)

a. Students excluded from the provisional scholarship rankings who do not intend to lodge a complaint, in accordance with art. 17(3) “Provisional rankings”. 

b. Students excluded from the definitive accommodation service and scholarship rankings, in accordance with art. 17(5) “Definitive rankings”. 

c. Students transferring courses for whom the University recognises an insufficient number of credits to maintain eligibility for the scholarship, in accordance with art. 15(4). 

d. Students who do not complete their enrolment by 3 April 2026, in accordance with art. 15. 

e. Students whose benefits have been withdrawn following a financial or merit assessment, including for previous academic years. 

f. Students enrolled in the additional semester who do not comply with the provisions of art. 34(6.1) “Allocation and use of the accommodation service - additional semesters - special cases”; 

g. Students whose benefits have been withdrawn because of an offence committed in the Residence in accordance with the Internal Regulations for Residences. 

# 3. Students who lose their right to residence due to the withdrawal of benefits in accordance with the articles of the Internal Regulations for University Residences who will not benefit from the possibility of applying for the accommodation service.

Benefits will be withdrawn in accordance with the combined provisions of this art. 35 and art. 38 “Withdrawal of Scholarship and Accommodation Service”.

SECTION XI 

# FINAL

# PROVISIONS

# ART. 36 POLICY PURSUANT TO ARTICLES 12, 13 AND 14 OF REGULATION (EU) NO. 679 OF 27 APRIL 2016 OF THE EUROPEAN PARLIAMENT AND OF THE COUNCIL ON THE PROTECTION OF INDIVIDUALS WITH REGARD TO PERSONAL DATA PROCESSING AND THE FREE MOVEMENT OF SUCH DATA

EDISU Piemonte processes personal data and is considered a Data Controller under the Personal Data Protection Regulation (EU) 27 April 2016, no. 679 (hereinafter, more briefly the “Regulation” or “GDPR”) and Legislative Decree No. 196 of 30 June 2003 (hereinafter, the “Code”). 

The purpose of this policy is to specify which personal data are processed, why they are recorded, and how they are used. 

# 1. DATA CONTROLLER

The data controller is EDISU Piemonte - Via Madama Cristina, 83 - 10126 - Turin (TO) Tax Code 97547570016 | VAT no. 06440290010. 

The Data Controller can be contacted at the e-mail address privacy@EDISU-piemonte.it, as well as by writing to the postal address indicated. 

# 2. PERSONAL DATA PROTECTION OFFICER

The Data Protection Officer, appointed pursuant to art. 37 of the Regulation, can be contacted at dpo@EDISU-piemonte.it 

# 3. LEGAL BASIS AND PURPOSE OF PERSONAL DATA PROCESSING

The processing of personal data is lawful if there is a valid legal basis. For the processing covered by this policy, the valid legal bases are as follows: 

Contract (art. 6(1)(b) of the Regulation): processing is necessary for the performance of a contract to which the data subject is party or for the performance of pre-contractual measures taken at the data subject's request; 

Legal Obligation (art. 6(1)(c) of the Regulation): processing is necessary for compliance with a legal obligation to which the data controller is subject; 

Public interest (art. 6(1)(e) of the Regulation): processing is necessary for the performance of a task carried out in the public interest or in the exercise of official authority vested in the controller; 

Obligation and/or right in relation to social protection (art. 9(2)(b) of the Regulation): processing is necessary for the purposes of fulfilling the obligations and exercising the specific rights of the data controller or the data subject in relation to social protection insofar as authorised by European Union or Member State law. 

Personal data will be processed in order to fulfil the obligations related to participation in the Notice of Competition (drawing up rankings, disbursement of benefits, etc.) and in order to carry out checks on the truthfulness and/or maintenance of the conditions (financial and merit) or of the status (by way of example, that of a beneficiary of international protection) that the participant self-certifies, including for the purpose of the withdrawal and consequent return of the benefits granted. 

Personal data will also be processed for the fulfilment of legal, accounting and tax obligations and for statistical purposes, the latter through communication to public bodies set up for this purpose. 

They will also be processed for the purposes of reporting and checks carried out by ministerial and regional bodies to verify the correct allocation of funding, in particular NRRP and ESF. 

Any additional, specific processing purposes, including as they arise, will be communicated with a different and more detailed policy, possibly accompanied by a request for the appropriate consent. 

# 4. PERSONAL DATA PROCESSED

EDISU Piemonte records, uses, and stores personal and contact data (e.g. name and surname, citizenship, telephone number, postal and e-mail address, tax code, family, and other personal identification data) communicated directly by the interested party when filling in and submitting the application for participation in the Notice of Competition. 

To provide the benefits referred to in the Notice of Competition, EDISU Piemonte also processes information relating to financial status, student career, status as a disabled person or beneficiary of international protection. This information is also communicated directly by the data subject. For a more precise identification of the types of personal data to be processed, please refer to the content of this Notice of competition and the information required by it for the submission of the relevant application. 

Lastly, EDISU Piemonte will process data not directly communicated by the data subject but received from institutional third parties (Agenzia delle Entrate, University attended, other Universities, etc.) from which these have been requested to carry out checks on the truthfulness and/or maintenance of the conditions and status self-certified by the participant. 

# 5. RECIPIENTS OR CATEGORIES OF RECIPIENTS OF PERSONAL DATA

To pursue the purposes stated in this Policy, the personal data will be disclosed to employees and collaborators of the Data Controller in their capacity as Authorised processors. 

The personal data will also be communicated to Companies/Professional firms that provide assistance and/or consultancy services to the Data Controller in accounting, administrative, tax, legal and financial matters, as well as to third-party service providers to whom such communication is necessary to fulfil the services covered by the Notice of Competition. 

These parties will process the data in their capacity as Data Processors. 

The Data Controller may also communicate personal data to administrative, institutional and/or judicial authorities (by way of example, Agenzia delle Entrate, Piedmont Universities, Guardia di Finanza, Regional Observatory for Universities and for the Right to University Study, National Association of Agencies for the Right to University Study, etc.) and to any other subject to whom communication is obligatory by law and/or for the fulfilment of the purposes indicated in this policy. 

These parties will process the data in their capacity as independent Data controllers. 

The full list of recipients of personal data is available on request from the Data Controller. 

# 6. USE OF AUTOMATED DECISION-MAKING PROCESSES

EDISU Piemonte uses automated decision-making processes in accordance with art. 22 of the Regulation for the allocation of points and the related ranking position. Pursuant to the above-mentioned article, the Data controller shall implement appropriate measures to protect the rights, freedoms and legitimate interests of the data subject, at least the right to obtain human intervention on the part of the data controller, to express their opinion, and to contest the decision. 

# 7. DISSEMINATION OF PERSONAL DATA

EDISU Piemonte does not disseminate personal data. The rankings can only be consulted on the personal Online Helpdesk page (by clicking on “Ranking” in the “Scholarship” section). 

# 8. PERSONAL DATA STORAGE TIME

The personal data contained in the application form, in attached documents, or subsequently transmitted and/or acquired, including at the initiative of E.DI.S.U PIEMONTE, will be stored for the time foreseen by the storage and disposal plan drawn up pursuant to Legislative Decree No. 42 of 22 January 2004 (“Cultural Heritage and Landscape Code”). 

# 9. NATURE OF PROVISION OF PERSONAL DATA AND CONSEQUENCES OF A REFUSAL TO DO SO

The provision of data is necessary for the awarding of points and the related ranking. Failure to provide data will therefore result in the impossibility of obtaining the benefits included in the Notice of Competition. 

# 10. TRANSFER OF PERSONAL DATA TO THIRD COUNTRIES OR INTERNATIONAL ORGANISATIONS

For the purposes listed in this Policy, personal data may be transferred to countries within or outside the European Union. In such cases, EDISU Piemonte will ensure that appropriate safeguards are in place to protect personal data in accordance with the requirements of the Regulation (arts. 44-50). 

# 11. RIGHTS GRANTED TO THE DATA SUBJECT

b) [letter omitted as not applicable to the processing indicated in this policy];
